*Certified Credstick								Legal*

Cash for the late 21<sup>st</sup> century. A certified credstick is not registered to any specific person – the electronic funds encoded on it belong to the holder, requiring no special ID or authorisation to use. The bad news is that you can be physically mugged, any money you have on your credstick jacked and rolled. The good news is that certified credsticks are completely untraceable. They’re not even wireless – you have to slot them into a universal data connector to transfer cash onto or off of them. This makes them enduringly popular with shadowrunners and the Mr Johnsons who love to hire them.

Each type of credstick can only hold up to a certain amount of money, listed below. This is the maximum amount it can carry, not the amount it always has on it – so don’t get excited when you see a gold credstick until you’ve slotted it and checked its balance.

|**Credstick**|**Max Value**|**Cost**|
| :- | :- | :- |
|**Standard**|5000|5¥|
|**Silver**|20,000|20¥|
|**Gold**|100,000|100¥|
|**Platinum**|500,000|500¥|

*Online Banking Account							Legal*

Online banking accounts can be accessed at any time via your commlink. Transactions require passcode or biometric verification to be authorised. The good news in no one can (physically) steal your bank account and hacking credit accounts often requires a run to Zurich Orbital or something equally suicidal. The bad news in that digital transactions leave a “paper trail” that, while it can be hidden or concealed, is entirely too traceable for serious criminal activities. Each account must be registered to a particular (usually fake) SIN, unless the account is handled by an anonymous underworld banking service (with its own risks and complications). The cost of banking services is included in your lifestyle costs if you’ve got a Low Lifestyle or better – otherwise you’ll need to keep all your money on credsticks.

<a name="_hlk204589980"></a>*Public Transportation Monthly Pass				50¥		Legal*

You have a monthly pass to access public transportation in your city. This includes bus, subway, ferry or any combination of them. This means, from most places within the city you have transportation access to your destination, with the caveat that it’s not as fast as you make like it.
### **Clothing**
In 2075, you’d have to be crazy to consider walking outside with just a tee-shirt and jeans, even in some of the nicer parts of the Sprawl. You need protection: from the acid rain, from air pollution, from ultraviolent radiation from the completely fragged ozone layer and, of course, from random street violence.
#### **Standard Clothing**
*Armoured Casualwear			Armour 6			450¥		Legal*

Lightweight ballistic fibre weave makes these garments almost impossible to detect as armour. It doesn’t provide as much protection as real armour, but it’s available in a wide variety of styles.

*Armoured Team Jersey			Armour 6			750¥		Legal*

Because you never know whose turf you’re tailgating in. Available for most sports but most popular with urban brawl teams that traditionally have the rowdiest fans (read: most likely to riot). +1 Social limit for tests involving fans. -1 Social limit for tests involving fans of rival teams.

*Synthleather Jacket			Armour 4			200¥		Legal*

This waist-length jacket never goes out of style and even offers a modicum of protection. Just don’t expect it to stop bullets.

*Armoured Jacket			Armour 12			1,000¥		Legal*

The most popular armour solution on the streets comes in all styles imaginable. If offers good protection without catching too much attention. But don’t think of wearing one to a dinner party. While the thick jacket protects the body’s core, remember that being shot in the legs may mean you can’t escape and may end up double-tapped.

*Armoured Raincoat			Armour 9			2,000¥		Legal*

Waterproof and ugly yellow, this raincoat protects against more than getting wet with its concealed armour. Gain a +6 dice pool bonus against acid rain and any contact-vector chemical and toxin attacks. You do gain a +2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath.

*Athleisure Securware			Armour 6			550¥		Legal*

Keeping a well-toned ass from getting shot, a combination of spiderweave threads and ballistic fibre weave provide flexible and fashionable protection that fits in many casual social situations. Crafted with biofabrics, athleisureware provides information wirelessly on the wearer’s general health: body temperature, pulse rate, blood pressure and so on. Don’t forget the in-built music player.

*Athleisure Securware – Shockless	Armour 6			2,000¥		Legal*

In addition to the usual benefits of athleisure securware, this upgraded line also provides strong resistance to tasers and shocks. (The wearer gains a +6 dice pool bonus against electrical attacks.)

*Fashionable Fur Coat			Armour 0			2,400¥		Legal*

Thermal fibres and heat-retentive materials protect the wearer against Cold damage. Gain a +6 dice pool bonus against cold attacks. You do gain a +2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath.

*Feedback Armoured Casualwear	Armour 6			950¥		Legal*

This haptic clothing allows for a tactile component to an augmented reality experience. Lightweight ballistic fibre weave makes these garments almost impossible to detect as armour. It doesn’t provide as much protection as real armour, but it’s available in a wide variety of styles.

*Poncho - Acid-Rain Resistant		Armour 0			350¥		Legal*

Water-resistant, non-porous, impermeable and with a coating of neutralising agents protect you against acid rain and any contact-vector chemical and toxin attacks (add 1 to those resistance tests). However, it’s rather unfashionable – suffer a -1 Social Limit modifier while it is worn. You do gain a +2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath.

*Urban Explorer Jumpsuit		Armour 8			800¥		Legal*

Designed for couriers, athletes and freerunners, these colourful jumpsuits are well ventilated and breathable but surprisingly protective with lightweight densiplast and liquid reactive armour. Urban explorer jumpsuits feature a built-in music player and biomonitor.
#### **Concealable Clothing**
*Armour Vest				Armour 9			500¥		Legal*

This modern flexible-wrap vest is designed to be worn under regular clothing without displaying any bulk. A popular and cost-effective option.

*Form-Fitting Body Armour		Armour 10			2,600¥		Legal*

While armoured clothing is effective enough and armoured vests are fairly well hidden, it takes truly advanced craftsmanship to produce form-fitting body armour.

*Second Skin				Armour 6			12,000¥		Legal*

This is a sexy, sick, twisted version of body armour. Each piece of the Second Skin line is custom tailored for the user, which means that a shift in weight of as little as one or two kilos will make the armour lose its most amazing benefit. That benefit is the fact that it is, for all intents and purposes, invisible. The full body unitard is almost undetectable and includes a completely integrated ruthenium polymer system, which allows the wearer to change any or all aspects of the suit’s appearance.
#### **Might Raise an Eyebrow Wear**
*Armoured Ten-gallon Hat		Armour +1			50¥		Legal*

A high-crowned, wide-brimmed hat best know as the defining piece of attire for the North American cowboy. Back in fashion (according to some) this variant incorporated ballistic weave to keep your noggin’ intact.

*Armoured Trenchcoat			Armour 9			900¥		Legal*

This Wild West style duster has been consistently popular on the mean streets of the world’s sprawls for the past thirty years. Besides its protective traits, the armoured trenchcoat provides an additional -2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath. But let’s face it – people walking around in dark trenchcoats don’t exactly inspire feelings of trust and faith.

*Base Jump Wingsuit			Armour 6			600¥		Legal*

The wingsuit is a jumpsuit with wings between the arms and torso and a third wing between the legs. The suit has inflatable pressurised cells, which increase the surface area of the diver’s body and provide greater lift. The suit allows the user to fly longer distances horizontally while falling more slowly.

*PolyProtect Trenchcoat		Armour 9				3,000¥		Legal*

For those who face a variety of threats, the PolyProtect is an option that protects and informs. Gain a +2 dice pool bonus against cold, electrical, fire and contact-vector toxin attacks. With a wireless connection, information about the incoming damage type and its vector may be transmitted to AR in real-time. Besides its protective traits, the PolyProtect Trenchcoat provides an additional -2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath.

*The Salamander Coat			Armour 9			2,500¥		Legal*

Fire-retardant and heat resistant, this duster is sold in a colour range from tar black to ochre orange and mercury red. With an in-built thermal monitor with wireless capabilities, not only will it provide excellent protection from heat and raw flames (+6 dice pool bonus against heat and fire damage), but it can also accurately gauge the temperature being felt in a 3-D heat pattern to AR in real-time. Besides its protective traits, the Salamander Coat provides an additional -2 Concealability modifier to items completely hidden underneath.

*Bike Racing Armour			Armour 9			700¥		Legal*

It’s some of the most obvious armour out there, but it seems perfectly normal to anyone who has seen or heard you arrive on your bike. So, people will notice that you’re wearing it, but it won’t automatically make them suspect you’re up to something. This stuff comes in a variety of customisable colours with and without cycle brand logos or combat biker team slogans. It includes a helmet, which may have additional upgrades.

*Motorbike Helmet			Armour +2			300¥		Legal*

While it is certainly tough, the idea that this would protect your skull from major trauma after a crash at over 100 km/hr seems laughable. It also has Capacity 6 for being tricked out with accessories such as trode nets and vision enhancements.

*Wetsuit					Armour 0			400¥		Legal*

Worn to provide thermal protection while wet, it is usually made of foamed neoprene and is worn by surfers, divers, windsurfers and other engaged in water sports or other activities in or on the water. By default, it provides a +1 dice pool bonus against cold.
#### **Corporate and Fashionable**
*Armante Suit				Armour 8			2,500¥		Legal*

Always a leader in the armoured fashion field in terms of quality product. This is a high-fashion suit for the high-class gentleman. It both increases the Social Limit by 2 and provides a +1 dice pool modifier in the appropriate settings.

*Executive Business Suit		Armour 8				1,500¥		Legal*

A discreet armoured “power suit” is a popular choice among Mr Johnsons, faces and fixers looking for a little high-class protection coupled with style. It includes a concealable holster in the jacket.

*Trés Chic Clothing			Armour 0			1,000¥		Legal*

Effortlessly polished, smart and sophisticated, this clothing is high-quality with labels known as among the best in the fashion industry.
#### <a name="_hlk204589968"></a>**Blatant and Attention Drawing**
*Ballistic Mask				Armour 2			150¥		Legal*

The come in a variety of custom mouldings and pain jobs to get almost any look imaginable, but matte black classic sells the best. They have limits when they’re basic models to keep them functional, but once electronic systems are added, the possibilities are endless. Ballistic masks can take vision enhancements as well as any modification a helmet can take. Custom jobs are, naturally, more expensive.

*Blackout Catsuit			Armour 11			6,650¥		Legal*

This full-body, skin-tight armour leaves little to the imagination but requires a custom-fit. A shift in weight as little as one or two kilos can cause problems. It provides excellent mobility with a minimum visual profile. The inner layers capture or bleed heat, so the outer layers maintain a surface temperature equal to the surrounding air (+6 to Sneaking Tests against thermographic vision or thermal sensors). It includes a tight black hood (with little cat ears) that masks the face as well. Of course, it is just about the most obvious outfit you could possibly wear to announce that you are an intruder. The hood is equipped with an Audio Link, Audio Enhancement Rating 3 and a Spatial Recogniser.

*Ninja Suit				Armour 9			900¥		Legal*

This all-black specialised outfit is designed for stealth and covert operations. It consists of a black, loose-fitting garment that includes gloves, tabi (split-toe socks with reinforced soles) and a ballistic mask. It is designed for ease of movement and quietness while including spiderweave threads and ballistic fibre weave for protection. The forearm guards are simple, non-reflective dermaplast that can be used to block melee attacks, especially blades, turning blows away without actually cutting into you.

*Ruthenium Polymer Cloak		Armour 0			16,000¥		Forbidden Legality*

A hooded cloak infused with ruthenium polymer fibres. Originally developed for military snipers and spotters who needed to remain concealed and stationary for an extended period of time. The sensor suite that replicates the surroundings has difficulty adapting to the rippling of the cloak while the wearer is in motion. These cloaks are also sometimes used to conceal small, strategically important objects. The base modifier to a Perception Test to spot the wearer is –6 while stationary and -3 while moving.

*Veiled Chameleon Suit			Armour 8			2,250¥		Forbidden Legality*

This full-body suit has a smart ruthenium polymer coating over electrochromic threads supported by a sensor suite; the technology allows it to scan its surroundings and replicate the images at the proper perspectives. You can also change the colour or display text, images or patterns. A veiled chameleon suit is also armoured for the wearer’s protection. Add 2 to both the limit and the dice pool bonus of Sneaking Tests to hide. The wearer can also effectively “hide in plain sight”. It takes a Simple Action to change the settings on your electrochromic suit or a Bonus Action with wireless connection.
### **Melee Weapons**
Melee weapons are for ending the lives of people conveniently within arm’s reach. Some runners swear by them, especially those who prefer to kill silently or are afraid of hackers bricking their guns. The damage value of most melee weapons is based on the wielder’s Strength, modified by the weapon.
#### **Blades**
Use the Blades skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Blades is the wielder’s Physical Limit.

*Ceramic/Plasteel Knife		Reach -	(STR +1)P	AP-1		75¥		Legal*

Ceramic knives are lightweight and non-metallic that are primarily sold as specialty tools. Divers use them because they are resistant to saltwater corrosion and explosive defusing experts use them because they are non-metallic and will not trigger bombs with magnetic anomaly detectors. Plasteel knives share most characteristics with ceramic knives, including being undetectable to MAD scanners. They are most commonly handmade from scraps taken from machinery or vehicles. A few designs are mass manufactured but generally ceramic is the preferred medium due to superior edge retention under heavy use. Both are equally useful to a shadowrunner who wants to sneak a blade into a secure area.

*Claymore, Highland Forge	Reach 2	(STR +5)P	AP-4		4,500¥		Licence Restricted*

Quality killing in the classic Scottish fashion. An ideal accessory for the troll who thinks a regular sword makes a better toothpick. The Highland Forge Claymore comes with a classic leather scabbard to add that authentic look. The blade is custom-forged with a proprietary technique even the masters of Damascus would be unable to match.

*Collapsible Sword		Reach 1	(STR +2)P	AP-3		1,250¥		Licence Restricted*

This sword folds down to the size of a long knife, with a Concealability rating of -2 when collapsed rather than the standard +4 Concealability rating of a sword.

*Combat Axe			Reach 1	(STR +5)P	AP-4		4,000¥		Licence Restricted*

A two-handed tungsten-alloy monster, available single- or double-bladed. A hardened thrusting point on be concealed, spring-loaded, in the handle. While it may seem barbaric or primitive, the physical augmentations of 2075 can make an old-school weapon like a combat axe even deadlier than a firearm in the right hands. So go ahead, go medieval.

*Combat Knife			Reach -	(STR +2)P	AP-3		300¥		Legal*

A long, KA-BAR-style fighting knife with a blacked-out blade and a chisel point for punching through armour.

*Forearm Snap Blades		Reach -	(STR +2)P	AP-2		300¥		Licence Restricted*

Simply concealed under loose clothing, these are externally strapped on – painless to install or remove. The forearm sheath conceals three blade that can be extended or retracted with a Use Device Action.

*Lapel Dagger			Reach -	(STR +1)P	AP-1		100¥		Legal*

Small, flat, synthetic composite, non-metallic dagger made to slip underneath the lapel of a jacket or along the seam of an outfit. Low damage but high concealability (Concealability -4) and undetectable by MAD scanners.

*Katana				Reach 1	(STR +3)P	AP-3		1,000¥		Licence Restricted*

The legendary sword of the samurai. The katana has become synonymous not just with street samurai, but with shadowrunners in general, at least in the trids; they’ve got everyone packing a katana, from the decker to the mage. But being a silly cliché doesn’t make this blade any less dangerous or less helpful in a fight.

*Knife				Reach -	(STR +1)P	AP-1		10¥		Legal*

Your basic, all-purpose street cutter. It comes in a bewildering array of styles, colours and flavours, but the statistics don’t vary from one to the next. Ordinary knives are used by the poor, the desperate or the cautious as backup weapons.

*Monosword, Ares ‘One’		Reach 1	(STR +3)P	AP-4		1,500¥		Licence Restricted*

“There can be only One” is Ares latest slogan for this classic. This tool of the modernised street samurai features a monofilament line along the edge that provides incredible penetration potential.

*Nodachi, Nippon Steel		Reach 2	(STR +5)P	AP-4		4,500¥		Licence Restricted*

For those who crave a samurai-style extra long blade, the Nippon Steel Nodachi offers reach and power with style.

*Nunchaku			Reach 1	(STR +2)P	AP+0		75¥		Licence Restricted*

Thought to have its origin as an Okinawan farming tool, the nunchaku is comprised of two short sticks made of wood, metal or plastic, fastened together by a short length of chain or rope. When properly used, nunchaku can deliver a flurry of blows from a variety of angles. Nunchaku can also be used to choke opponents.

*Pole Arm			Reach 2	(STR +3)P	AP-2		1,000¥		Licence Restricted*

This is, at its very essence, a blade on the end of a very long stick. It usually features an axe-head, glaive, spear point or similar maiming implement. It’s not easy to handle and it’s just about impossible to conceal, but it’s popular both with trolls and with melee combatants looking to safely keep said large trolls at more than arm’s length.

*Rapier, Horizon-Flynn	Reach 1	(STR +2)P	AP-3			500¥		Licence Restricted*

Not every street samurai studies the art of kenjutsu. Some prefer the more elegant Flore del Liberi and thus choose the rapier over the common katana. Horizon and world-renowned bladesmith Dante Flynn have joined forces to create the ultimate tool for slipping past a flawed defence and finding a home in the heart of an enemy. The Horizon-Flynn blade is a slender composite designed for strength, flexibility and stability for maximum armour penetration.

*Sword				Reach 1	(STR +2)P	AP-2		300¥		Licence Restricted*

It’s sharp, it’s heavy and it will fragging cut you wide open. Available in a wide variety of styles (wakizashi, scimitar, machete, and so on and so forth), this one-handed blade is not as formidable as a katana but is substantially easier to hide.

*Swordcane			Reach 1	(STR +2)P	AP-2		500¥		Legal*

A hidden release on the cane allows you to draw out a short, rapier-style blade. Concealment modifiers are +0 for the whole cane and -6 to determine its true nature.

*Tanto				Reach -	(STR +2)P	AP-1		100¥		Legal*

A single or double edges blade roughly 30 centimetres long designed in the Heian period that is one of the most revered samurai blade in Japanese history, worn by feudal Japan’s samurai class.
#### **Clubs**
Use the Clubs skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Clubs is the wielder’s Physical Limit.

*Club				Reach 1	(STR +3)P	AP+0		30¥		Legal*

This telescoping club can be collapsed and it can be extended with a sharp flick of the wrist or a wireless signal. When retracted, it’s more easily concealed (Concealability 0 when retracted, +2 when extended). Reading the extendable baton is a Use Device action.

*Sap				Reach 0	(STR +2)P	AP+0		50¥		Legal*

Also called a blackjack, this is a small, springy club or a flat piece of iron in a flexible leather covering. It’s specially designed for concealment (Concealability -2).

This large, heavy stick is popular with magicians going for that traditional look. Available in composite, hardwood, high-carbon steel and other materials.

*Stun Baton			Reach 1	9S(elec)	AP-5		750¥		Licence Restricted*

A standard riot-control weapon, viewed as a tool and symbol of corporate-government oppressors but pragmatically useful to runners. It has ten charges and regains one charge per ten seconds when plugged in. If wireless is enabled, it recharged by induction, regaining one charge per full hour of wireless-enabled time.

*Stun Staff, Nemesis Arms	Reach 2	9S(elec)	AP-5		1,000¥		Licence Restricted*

Double-sided zapping power! The stun staff is basically a staff with stun batons on each end. They’re rather large and a bit ugly but they look quite intimidating in the hands of the guards at Shiawase HQ.

*Telescoping Staff		Reach 2	(STR+3)P	AP+0		350¥		Legal*

This is a metal and composite staff than can telescope down to a reasonable size, one that can be concealed about as easily as a stun baton. It can be extended and lock in place by whirling it at the correct speed and angle and twisting the grip or via a wireless signal. Reading the telescoping staff is a Use Device Action.
#### **Fist Weapons**
Use the Unarmed Combat skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Fist Weapons is the wielder’s Physical Limit.

*Knucks			Reach -	(STR+1)P	AP+0			100¥		Licence Restricted*

These may be traditional fist-load weapons like brass knuckles or modern “Hardliner gloves” with a thin layer of densiplast located along the knuckles and the edge of the hand. Either way, they substantially boost the impact of a punch, making it potentially deadly.

*Shock Gloves		Reach -	9S(elec)	AP-5			550¥		Licence Restricted*

These electrically insulated gloves have a wire mesh that discharges electric current with a punch or a simple touch. The gloves deal electrical damage and are good for ten charges before they need to be plugged in and recharged (at a rate of one charge per ten seconds). If wireless is enabled, it recharged by induction, regaining one charge per full hour of wireless-enabled time.
### **Projectile and Throwing Weapons**
These weapons are primarily muscle-powered, although some might use simple mechanical assistance for added distance or speed.
#### **Bows**
Use the Archery skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Bows is listed in the weapon description.

Bow		Rating 2		Accuracy: Physical	4P	AP+0		200¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 3		Accuracy: Physical	5P	AP+0		300¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 4		Accuracy: Physical	6P	AP-1		400¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 5		Accuracy: Physical	7P	AP-1		500¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 6		Accuracy: Physical	8P	AP-1		600¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 7		Accuracy: Physical	9P	AP-1		700¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 8		Accuracy: Physical	10P	AP-2		800¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 9		Accuracy: Physical	11P	AP-2		900¥	Legal

Bow		Rating 10		Accuracy: Physical	12P	AP-2		1,000¥	Legal

Arrow		Rating 1-10						Rating x2¥		Legal

This could be a traditional longbow of fiberglass or wood, or possibly a modern compound-and-pulley bow. Both are archaic and rare weapons on the streets of 2075 and both have the advantage of being hacker-proof. Reloading a bow takes a Simple Action.

Bows have Rating that indicate the minimum Strength you need to use that weapon. When attacking with a bow, a character whose Strength is less than the Strength minimum suffer a 3 dice pool penalty per point below the minimum; this penalty reflects the difficulty they have in pulling the bow and nocking an arrow.

The weapon’s Rating is also used to determine its range and damage (maximum Rating is 10). Use the lowest value of your Strength, the bow’s Rating or the arrow Rating for range and damage when attacking a target, because your average Rating 10 titanium-sheathed beryllium-allow bow tends to turn wood or fibreglass arrows into powder when they hit a target.
#### **Crossbows**
Use the Archery skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Crossbows is listed in the weapon description.

*Light Crossbow		Accuracy: 7		5P	AP-1		300¥		Legal*

*Medium Crossbow	Accuracy: 7		7P	AP-2		500¥		Licence Restricted*

*Heavy Crossbow	Accuracy: 7		10P	AP-3		1,000¥		Licence Restricted*

*Crossbow Bolt								5¥		Legal*

Modern crossbows are equipped with automatic reloading devices, so unless you’re using a museum piece, reloading doesn’t require a Ready Weapon action. Crossbows have internal magazines holding up to 4 bolts. Crossbows are available in Light, Medium and Heavy sizes.
#### **Throwing Blades**
Use the Thrown Weapons skill to wield these weapons. The Accuracy for Throwing Blades is listed in the weapon description.

*Throwing Blades	Accuracy: Physical	 (STR+1)P	AP-1	25¥		Licence Restricted*

A wide variety of shapes and sizes of aerodynamically balanced, specially weighted, muscle-powered throwing weapons are available, from throwing spikes to darts to kunai and shuriken. A character can ready (Agi/2) of these blades with one Ready Weapon action.
### **Tasers**
Tasers are legal to carry and a great choice for non-lethally incapacitating someone. Tasers, like other electrical weapons, have a flat Armour Penetration value of -5 and deal electricity damage. Use the Handguns skill to fire a taser. Tasers can take only top-mounted accessories.

*Cavalier Safeguard	Accuracy: 5(6)	SA	6S(elec)	AP-5	6 (mag)	275¥	Legal*

A reliable self-defence weapon, this taser forgoes some wattage in each dart for a larger ammunition capacity and back this with a top-mounted laser for increased accuracy for a less skilled shooter. It still looks sufficiently enough like a pistol to still intimidate targets who might scoff at a mere taser.

Activating or deactivating a laser sight is a Use Device action.

*Defiance EX Shocker	Accuracy: 4		SS	9S(elec)	AP-5	4 (mag)	250¥	Legal*

*(in melee)		Accuracy: Physical	8S(elec)		AP-5	Reach 0*

This heavy-duty taser fires up to 4 darts that trail wires up to 20 metres long. The wired connection to the battery allows for a more powerful shock. Most modern tasers use wireless darts, so the Defiance EX Shocker is an exception. It also features contacts that allow it to be used as a stun weapon in melee.

A successful hit with an active wireless connection informs you of the status of the target’s basic health.

*Tiffani-Defiance Protector	Accuracy: 5(6)   SA	7S(elec)	AP-5	3 (mag)	400¥	Legal*

A sleek taser designed to accessorise well with women’s fashions, with the added benefit of geckogrip to allow it to be set anywhere that is comfortable on the body and a sleek top-mounted laser sight for quick targeting. This is a perfect choice to go with the immortal little black dress, stored under the dashboard of a car or put next to the bed for a good night’s sleep.

`	`Having trouble holding on to your gun? Then maybe you shouldn’t have one. But if that’s not an option, try gecko grip, which makes your piece stick in your hand like, well, a gecko hanging on a wall. The mod gives a +6 dice pool bonus on any test to see if a character keeps their grip on the gun. It can also be used to stick the gun to your jacket, back or roof of your car.

The darts of this taser contain wireless capacitors, meaning that the Pulsar eliminates the need for cumbersome wires. As a trade-off, it is slightly less powerful than the EX Shocker, although it can fire faster. It lacks the EX Shocker’s melee contacts.

A successful hit with an active wireless connection informs you of the status of the target’s basic health.
### **Hold-Outs**
Hold-out pistols are very concealable and are perfect for sneaking into a meet or wearing as a back-up piece. They don’t have much else going for them, being both weak and inaccurate. Use the Handguns skill when firing a hold-out pistol. Hold-outs can’t take mounted accessories.

|**Range**|**Short**|**Medium**|**Long**|**Extreme**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**Hold-Outs**|0-5m|6-15m|16-30m|31-50m|

*Colt New Model Revolver	Accuracy: 6	SA	5P		AP+0	5 (cy)	180¥	Licence Restricted*

The New Model Revolver is Colt’s return to the small-revolver market, launched with a marketing campaign aimed at young homeowners and small security firms. The New Model is manufactured in a variety of small calibre and is largely of conventional design. The cylinder uses a simple left-side drop to allow rapid reloading with the appropriate manufacturer-approved speed loader. This model is only produced at Colt’s Connecticut facility and has largely remained rare outside of northeastern UCAS. Inside the UCAS, citizens can be proud to purchase from one of their homegrown success stories. Trust the quality of a proven manufacturer. Trust the Legend.

*Fichetti Tiffani Needler		Accuracy: 5	SA	8P(f)		AP+5	4 (c)	1,000¥	Licence Restricted*

Designed to appeal to social climbers and debutantes, the Tiffani Needler is available in a wide variety of colours and styles. It also has a special colour-changing coating that can be manipulated via wireless signal. This is useful to make sure your gun matches with your shoes or your handbag. The Needler can only fire flechette rounds. You can change the colours of the Tiffani Needler with a Use Device Action.

*Raecor Sting			Accuracy: 4	SS	6P(f)		AP+5	5 (c)	500¥	Licence Restricted*

The Sting is commonly referred to as a “lemon-squeezer” design, meaning the barrel protrudes from between the firer’s index and middle fingers and the gun is fired by simply making a fist. The circular magazine rotates and automatically loads the next mini-flechette round. Constructed entirely from polyresins, the Sting cannot be detected by magnetic weapon detection systems.

*Streetline Special		Accuracy: 4	SA	6P		AP+0	6 (c)	120¥	Licence Restricted*

Popular among society’s dregs, the Streetline Special is a small, lightweight weapon made of composite materials. Magnetic Anomaly Detectors (MAD Scanners) suffer a -2 dice pool penalty to detect it.

*Walther Palm Pistol		Accuracy: 4	SS/BF	7P		AP+0	2 (b)	180¥	Licence Restricted*

This is a classic double-barreled derringer in an over-under barrel combination. It packs a punch for its size, but on the downside has one of the most diminutive “magazine” capacities on the market – just one bullet per barrel. Both barrels can be fired at once as a short burst (for a -1 Defence modifier instead of the normal -2 for Burst Fire).
### **Light Pistol**
Light pistols are highly accurate and fairly concealable, occupying a comfortable middle ground between Hold-outs and Heavy Pistols. They’re extremely common the streets. Use the Handguns skill when firing a light pistol. Light pistol can take top- and barrel-mounted accessories.

|**Range**|**Short**|**Medium**|**Long**|**Extreme**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**Light Pistols**|0-5m|6-15m|16-30m|31-50m|

*Beretta 201T			Accuracy: 6	SA/BF	6P		AP+0	21 (c)	210¥	Licence Restricted*

This light sidearm is used by many security professionals. It is capable of burst fire. Since the 201T is classified as a light pistol without further limitations, it is quite popular with security agencies in countries where heavy pistols and machine pistols are hard to come by legally. Semi-automatic burst using the Beretta 201T require a Simple Action. The weapon includes a detachable shoulder stock.

*Cavalier Arms Adder Slivergun	Accuracy: 5	SA	8P(f)		AP+5	20 (c)	320¥	Licence Restricted*

Oddly enough, this gun was developed as a lightweight personal protection weapon for a mail-delivery corp. Management’s logic was that flechette ammo would be more effective against aggressive dogs and similar paracritters while being less intimidating to customers. It is reminiscent of a pared-down Ares Viper Slivergun. With the modification of an aftermarket silencer, this gun is exceptionally handy for sneaking into a location and striking while the target’s guard is down.

*Colt Agent Special		Accuracy: 5	SA	8P		AP+0	8 (c)	250¥	Licence Restricted*

The Agent Special has been one of Colt’s bestsellers since its introduction over a century ago and continuing updates and upgrades keep it more than relevant. The weapon’s large calibre makes it popular with shooters who prefer hitting power over range. The short barrel also reduces the round’s penetrative power but the ability to use the same ammunition as a heavy pistol means that some organisations are turning to this steady performer to simplify their logistics.

*Colt America L36		Accuracy: 7	SA	7P		AP+0	11 (c)	320¥	Licence Restricted*

A venerable pistol with a great reputation. This basic firearm is cheap, easily concealed and nearly ubiquitous. A perfect throwaway weapon.

*Fichetti Executive Action	Accuracy: 6	SA/BF	7P		AP+0	18 (c)	300¥	Licence Restricted*

“Manage your danger with Executive Action!” is the latest in a long series of taglines for this pistol, which incorporates a burst-fire option as standard. With no other truly compelling features, marketing is what this firearm mostly has going for it but that appears to be all it needs to keep selling well.

*Fichetti Security 600		Accuracy: 6(7)	SA	7P		AP+0	30 (c)	350¥	Licence Restricted*

A light sidearm for security forces, this weapon’s highly efficient feeding mechanism allows it a thirty-round magazine. The Fichetti Security 600 comes with a detachable folding stock and under-barrel mounted laser sight.
> `	`*Laser Sight*
\*\
`	`This device uses a laser beam to project a visible dot (in your choice of colours) on the target. This increases the weapon’s Accuracy by 1 and grants a +1 dice pool bonus, which is not cumulative with smartlink modifiers. The laser sight can be attached to either the underbarrel or top mount. Activating or deactivating a laser sight is a Use Device action.
> `	`*Folding Stock*
\*\
`	`This is a stock. That folds into the weapon. Got it? It provides 1 point of recoil compensation – but only, of course, when it is out and braced against the user’s shoulder. It must be installed in the stock slot and requires a Simple Action to move in or out.

*SK Katzbalger			Accuracy: 6(8)	SA	7P		AP+0	12 (c)	1,750¥	Licence Restricted*
> `	`*Electronic Firing*
\*\
`	`With this modification, most of the weapon’s moving parts are removed so that it can fire electronically, meaning that an electrical signal detonates the bullet’s propellant. This provides 1 point of recoil compensation and a -1 dice pool modifier to sound-based Perception Tests when trying to locate where the weapon is being fired from. The weapon still includes a loading mechanism that moves the bullet into the chamber and it requires caseless ammunition.
> `	`*Trigger Removal*
\*\
`	`Sometimes the time it takes to move a finger is too long. Sometimes the pressure of squeezing a trigger is enough to throw off the precision of a long range shot. This is the modification for those times. A smartgun system is necessary for trigger removal, since the gun requires a command delivered wirelessly or through an optical cable to fire. This modification adds +1 Accuracy but is not cumulative with any other modification that adds to Accuracy other than the requisite smartlink. Wireless triggering requires wireless to be turned on. In case you were wondering.
> `	`*Smartgun System, Internal*
\*\
`	`This connects a firearm to the user’s smartlink. Incorporating a small camera and a laser range finder, the smartlink keeps track of ammunition, heat buildup and material stress. You can mentally switch between gun modes, eject a clip and fire the gun without pulling the trigger. The camera lets you shoot around corners without exposing yourself to return fire (at a -3 dice pool penalty). The system makes use of advanced calculation software, allowing for precisely calculated trajectories and high precision over any distance.

Developed for a niche market, this light pistol has had most of the moving parts removed to increase reliability and firing electronically without a trigger, while connected to the wielder with an internal smartgun system. The smartlink provides a +1 dice pool bonus to all attacks with the weapon or +2 if you’re using an augmentation for which you paid Essence.
### **Heavy Pistol**
Heavy Pistols are powerful sidearms that are a good compromise between concealability and firepower. When you shoot a heavy pistol, you use the Handguns skill. Heavy pistols can take top- and barrel-mounted accessories.

|**Range**|**Short**|**Medium**|**Long**|**Extreme**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**Heavy Pistols**|0-5m|6-20m|21-40m|41-60m|

*Ares Predator V		Accuracy: 5(7)	SA	8P		AP-1	15 (c)	725¥	Licence Restricted*

The newest iteration of the most popular handgun in the world, especially with mercenaries and shadowrunners. Upgraded with improved ergonomics and handling features, the Ares Predator V includes a smartgun system. Some say that the Ares Predator V isn’t better than other guns in its class, but no one can argue that it has better brand recognition.
> `	`*Smartgun System, Internal*
\*\
`	`This connects a firearm to the user’s smartlink. Incorporating a small camera and a laser range finder, the smartlink keeps track of ammunition, heat buildup and material stress. The camera lets you shoot around corners without exposing yourself to return fire (at a -3 dice pool penalty). This venerable sidearm is the Ares Predator’s primary competition as the world’s toughest heavy pistol. It offers a built-in top-mounted laser sight and is slightly cheaper.

*Cavalier Deputy		Accuracy: 6	SA	7P		AP-1	7 (c)	225¥	Licence Restricted*

With the return of Western aesthetics in fashion, the Deputy has become a choice for modern-day urban cowboys and gunslingers. Less punishing to the wrist and carrying a seven-chamber cylinder, this pistol is a choice competitor to the Ruger Super Warhawk.

*Colt Government 2046		Accuracy: 6	SA	7P		AP-1	14 (c)	425¥	Licence Restricted*

This government-issue weapon, styled after the legendary Colt M1911a1 uses an electrically induced spark to detonate the bullet’s propellants. The removal of the most moving parts from the firing mechanism gives this weapon a reputation for being exceptionally reliable.
> *Electronic Firing*
\*\

*Colt Manhunter			Accuracy: 5(6)	SA	8P		AP-1	16 (c)	700¥	Licence Restricted*

Falling a distant third place between the constant advertising battle between the Savalette Guardian and the Ares Predator V, Colt has taken a different track with the latest iteration of the Manhunter. Shifting everything back to traditional mechanical mechanisms with the exception of a holographic sight. The worst a hacker can do is make you slightly less accurate with this gun and that appeals to a lot of the less technologically-minded consumers. While production numbers are currently significantly smaller than its competitors, it is still readily available and a common sight on the streets.

*Savalette Guardian		Accuracy: 5 (7)	SS/BF\*	8P		AP-1	12 (c)	870¥	Licence Restricted*

This heavily chromed street monster of a pistol has been popular in the shadows for over two decades. A heavy pistol with an integrated smartgun link, an internal micro-gyro recoil absorption system and the option for burst firing, it’s a very reasonable weapon for an experienced owner who expects to be in heavy combat. Recoil Compensation 1.

*Remington Roomsweeper	Accuracy: 4	SA	7P		AP-1	8 (m)	250¥	Licence Restricted*

This is really more of a short-barrelled shotgun than a pistol.

*Ruger Super Warhawk		Accuracy: 5	SS	9P		AP-2	6 (cy)	400¥	Licence Restricted*

This revolver is as loud as a jet liner and twice as shiny. It’s also one of the scariest handguns in the world. The cased ammo variant is popular for the sheer thrill of swinging open the cylinder gate one handed and dumping spent brass.
### **Machine Pistol**

*Shiawase Arms Torrent	Accuracy: 4(6)	SA/BF/FA	10P	RC 5	AP-2	76 (c)	4,750¥	Licence Restricted*

For the discerning security professional, this assault rifle comes equipped with an array of modifications to reduced recoil, increase accuracy, increase ammo capacity and increase safety. With limited production runs, this firearm is used by elite corp HTR (High Threat Response) squads.
> `	`*Gas-vent System III*
\*\
`	`Gas-vent recoil compensation systems are barrel-mounted accessories that vent a weapon’s barrel gases as a specific vector to counter muzzle climb. Once installed, a gas-vent cannot be removed. Gas-vent systems provides a number of points of Recoil Compensation equal to their rating.
> `	`*Shock Pad*

`	`A shock-absorbing pad is situated on the rigid stock of a rifle, shotgun or heavy weapon and provides 1 point of recoil compensation.
> `	`*Foregrip*

`	`This is a handle you put on in the front of the weapon to give you a sturdier grip. It can be mounted on the barrel or underneath slots and it cannot be used on Pistols and Hold-outs. It provides 1 point of Recoil Compensation and adds 1 to the Concealability of the weapon to which it’s attached.  
> `	`*Smartgun System, Internal*

This connects a firearm to the user’s smartlink. Incorporating a small camera and a laser range finder, the smartlink keeps track of ammunition, heat buildup and material stress. You can mentally switch between gun modes, eject a clip and fire the gun without pulling the trigger. The camera lets you shoot around corners without exposing yourself to return fire (at a -3 dice pool penalty). The system makes use of advanced calculation software, allowing for precisely calculated trajectories and high precision over any distance.
> `	`*Electronic Firing*
\*\
`	`With this modification, most of the weapon’s moving parts are removed so that it can fire electronically, meaning that an electrical signal detonates the bullet’s propellant. This provides 1 point of recoil compensation and a -1 dice pool modifier to sound-based Perception Tests when trying to locate where the weapon is being fired from. The weapon still includes a loading mechanism that moves the bullet into the chamber and it requires caseless ammunition.
> `	`*Trigger Removal*
\*\
`	`Sometimes the time it takes to move a finger is too long. Sometimes the pressure of squeezing a trigger is enough to throw off the precision of a long range shot. This is the modification for those times. A smartgun system is necessary for trigger removal, since the gun requires a command delivered wirelessly or through an optical cable to fire. This modification adds +1 Accuracy but is not cumulative with any other modification that adds to Accuracy other than the requisite smartlink. Wireless triggering requires wireless to be turned on. In case you were wondering.
> `	`*Advanced Safety System*

It’s always good to make sure your weapon only goes off when you want it to. The advanced safety system works along with your smartlink (meaning that you need a smartlink to have one of these) to make sure only an authorized user fires the gun. There are a few ways to pull this off – one is to have biometric scanners in the grip or butt of the weapon or the system can scan for an authorized RFID tag to PAN within 1 meter of the weapon. If the authorized user(s) is present or holding the gun, it’ll be ready to fire. If not, no dice.
> `	`*Imaging Scope*

`	`These classic scopes are attached to the top mount; attaching or removing them takes only a Simple Action. Imaging scopes include a micro camera and vision magnification and they have a Capacity of 3 to hold vision enhancements.
> `	`*Extended Clip II*

Sometimes the job calls for the ability to fire more shots without taking time to reload. That is what an extended clip is for. A Rating 2 Extended Clip adds 100% more rounds to the gun’s capacity. The downside is that it makes the gun a bit harder to hide (+1 Concealability). More of an accessory that a modification, an Extended Clip does not use any modification slots.
### **Sniper Rifles**
Use the Longarms skills when firing sniper rifles. Firearm enthusiasts will be the first to tell you that sport and hunting rifles are technically not sniper rifles but they are similar enough in terms of game statistics to be included here rather than in their own section. Sniper rifles can take top-, barrel- and underbarrel-mounted accessories.

|**Range**|**Short**|**Medium**|**Long**|**Extreme**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**Sniper Rifle**|0-50m|51-350m|351-800m|801-1,500m|

*Marlin 3041 BL		Accuracy: 5	SA	10P	RC -	AP-3	6 (m)	1,100¥	Licence Restricted*

A classic rifle for traditional shooters, the 3041’s level action has been extensively reengineered to meet the toughest reliability standards, as shown by its selection by Illinois’ Department of Revenue as its issue long arm. The rifle’s barrel and action have been protected by Marlin’s proprietary anti-corrosion treatment to create an heirloom sure to last through generations of use. It comes with an imaging scope with vision magnification.

*Pioneer 60		Accuracy: 5	SS	10P	RC -	AP-1	5 (m)	500¥	Licence Restricted*

Morgan Boone’s been the face of the Kentucky Long Rifle Company for decades and his Pioneer 60 is a household staple in rural areas across the CAS and UCAS even if his company refuses to sell it to anyone in the NAN. Simple but effective, it’s a rugged design that’s perfect for someone that just wants to get out of the house for a weekend of drinking beer and popping off a few rounds into the local fauna.

*Remington 950		Accuracy: 7	SS	12P	RC -	AP-4	5 (m)	2,100¥	Licence Restricted*

This high-powered bolt-action hunting rifle features classic wooden furnishings and a top-mounted imaging scope that has kept it popular with hunters for several decades. It cannot mount underbarrel accessories.

*Ruger 101		Accuracy: 6	SA	11P	RC (1)	AP-3	8 (m)	1,300¥	Licence Restricted*

This futuristic-looking, gas-operated sporting rifle is the favourite weapon for many professional hunters and hobbyists. It features a built-in imaging scope and a rigid stock with shock pad.
### **Shotguns**
Use the Longarms skills when firing shotguns. The stats for these shotguns are for normal slug rounds. When firing shot, use the special rules for shotguns and flechette ammo. Shotguns can take top-, barrel- and underbarrel-mounted accessories.

|**Range**|**Short**|**Medium**|**Long**|**Extreme**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**Shotgun (slug)**|0-10m|11-40m|41-80m|81-150m|
|**Shotgun (shot)**|0-15m|16-30m|31-45m|46-60m|

*Beretta Northstar	Accuracy: 4(6)	SA	11P	RC -	AP-1	6(m)x2	2,000¥	Licence Restricted*

With its innovative dual-magazine design, the Northstar is quickly becoming the bullpup shotgun of choice for urban scenarios. Able to toggle between two different types of ammunition, the Northstar doubles the user’s tactical choices as well as their ammunition capacity. Just sixty-six centimetres long, the Northstar is ideally suited to navigate the type of restricted terrain today’s professional finds in the modern sprawl.

Standard accessories: Additional magazine (side), smartgun system (internal)

*Defiance T-250		Accuracy: 4	SS/SA	10P	RC -	AP-1	5 (m)	450¥	Licence Restricted*

A common sight on the mean street when things escalate beyond pistols and knives, this semi-automatic shotgun is available in either a normal-length or short-barrelled version. It is gas operated but also features a secondary pump action for situations where preventing jams is more important that quickly firing a second shot. The short-barrelled version has the concealability of +4, the range of a heavy pistol and a DV of 9P.

*PJSS Model 55		Accuracy: 6	SS	11P	RC -	AP-1	2 (b)	1,000¥	Licence Restricted*

This is a weapon of classic style for a classic sport. Produced only in small numbers, it’s renowned among European hunters and trap shooters as a precise and prestigious weapon. The weapon’s rigid stock comes equipped with an integrated shock pad. Both barrels can be shot at once as a short burst with only a -1 Defence Modifier.

*Remington 990		Accuracy: 4	SA	11P	RC -	AP-1	8 (c)	950¥	Licence Restricted*

Whether you’re on a budget and need a good solid boom-stick or looking for a nice base weapon to modify the drek out of, you can’t go wrong with the Remington 990. A solid, no-frills design, the 990 has been in steady production for almost seventy years and is widely available in almost every part of the world. Professionals appreciate the weapon’s ruggedness and reliability right out of the box while novices appreciate its ease of use and low cost. The 990 comes standard with a top rail mount and a smaller mount near the fore-stock for accessories.
### **Ammunition**
Ammunition is defined by type (regular, gel, APDS, etc.) class of firearm (light pistol, heavy pistol, assault rifle, etc) and as cased and caseless. Unless indicated otherwise in its description, a gun can fire cased or caseless ammo, but not both.

For simplicity, each kind of gun can trade ammo with another of its class: for example, all heavy pistols can share ammo.

An ammunition type’s Damage Modifier and AP Modifier are added to the weapon’s usual DV and AP.

*APDS rounds		DV+0		AP-4			(per 10 rounds)	200¥	Forbidden Legality*

These are military-grade armour piercing rounds – their full name is armour piercing discarding sabot. They are designed to travel at high velocities and punch through personal body armour. They are highly restricted and hard to acquire.

*Flechette rounds	DV+2		AP+5			(per 10 rounds)	65¥	Licence Restricted*

The payload of a flechette round is made up of tiny, tightly packed metal slivers. The round breaks up and shatters on impact, becoming a tumbling hail of shrapnel. Flechette rounds are devastating against unprotected targets, but not as effective against hardened armour.

*Gel rounds		DV Stun	AP+1			(per 10 rounds)	25¥	Licence Restricted*

These less-lethal rounds use a hard, jelly-like substance that is a safer alternative to rubber bullets. They are often employed for riot control. Their usually semi-rigid slugs flatten on impact, dispersing their kinetic energy over a larger-than-normal area. Gel rounds inflict Stun damage. Gel rounds reduce the target’s Physical limit by 2 when checking for **Knockdown**.

*Hollow points		DV+1		AP+2			(per 10 rounds)	70¥	Licence Restricted*

Hollow point rounds have their tips indented, so they are designed to “mushroom” or expand on impact, becoming a hail of deadly fragments not unlike flechettes, although hollow points are a much older technology. Like flechettes, follow points work better on unarmoured targets and tend to flatten against armour.

*Regular ammo		DV+0		AP+0			(per 10 rounds)	20¥	Licence Restricted*

Also called ball or full metal jacket rounds, these solid slugs are useful for numerous applications (mainly killing things).

*Subsonic ammo		DV+0		AP+0			(per 10 rounds)	40¥	Forbidden Legality*

Subsonic ammunition features a lighter charge and a slightly smaller bullet than regular rounds. This slows the bullet’s muzzle velocity below the speed of sound, reducing the sound of the weapon being fired and making it easier to silence. Subsonic ammunition applies a -1 dice pool modifier on all Perception Tests to notice the weapon’s use or locate the firing position. This dice pool modifier increases to -6 if a silencer or sound suppressor is used (replacing the usual -4 bonus from silencers or sound suppressors). Increase all penalties due to range by 1.

*Taser Darts		DV+0		AP+0				(each)	5¥	Legal*

These darts are designed to be loaded into taser weapons.

*Spare Clip	[Not ammo, but you probably want it to hold the ammo]		5¥	Legal*

A spare clip comes unloaded by can hold the maximum rounds for the weapon. Each clip is specific to the weapon you buy it for. And yes, it’s technically a detachable box magazine, but the Cityspeak word for it is so popular these days that even the catalogs call them clips.
### **Firearm Accessories**

*Bipod			[Under Mount]						200¥	Legal*

This two-legged brace extends downward from the weapon, allowing it to be fired low to the ground with the user in a prone or sitting position. A bipod can be attached to the underbarrel mount of a weapon and provides 2 points of Recoil Compensation when properly deployed. Attaching a bipod takes one minute. Folding up or deploying a bipod is a Simple Action. Removing it is a Complex Action. *Wireless*: Folding up or deploying the bipod is a Bonus Action.

*Electronic Firing	[Barrel Mount]						1,000¥	Licence Restricted*

With this modification, most of the weapon’s moving parts are removed so that it can fire electronically, meaning that an electrical signal detonates the bullet’s propellant. This provides 1 point of recoil compensation and a -1 dice pool penalty to sound-based Perception Tests when trying to locate where the weapon is being fired from. Electronic firing is usually combined with trigger removal to further reduce the number of moving parts, but this is not mandatory. The weapon still includes a loading mechanism that moves the bullet into the chamber, and it requires caseless ammunition.

*Extended Clip									35¥	Legal*

Sometimes the job calls for the ability to fire more shots without taking time to reload. That is what an extended clip is for. A Rating 1 Extended Clip adds 50% more rounds to the gun’s capacity and a Rating 2 Extending Clip adds 100% more rounds. The downside is that it makes the gun a bit harder to hide (+1 Concealability per Rating). More of an accessory that a modification, an Extended Clip does not use any modification slots.

*Flashlight		[Top or Under Mount]*

Standard Flashlight								25¥	Legal

Low-Light Flashlight								25¥	Legal

Thermographic Flashlight							25¥	Legal

By 2075, most flashlights are long lasting and super bright. Durability and brightness depend on the size – the bulkier, the better. Flashlights are also available in low-light and infrared versions, reducing visibility modifiers for low-light and thermographic vision, respectively. A flashlight can also be mounted to a weapon’s top or under-barrel mount.

*Folding Stock		[Stock Mount]							Legal*

Standard									30¥

Motorised									100¥

This is a stock. That folds into the weapon. Got it? It provides 1 point of recoil compensation – but only, of course, when it is out and braced against the user’s shoulder. It must be installed in the stock slot and requires a Simple Action to move in or out. There is a motorised version that makes folding an unfolding it a Bonus Action with a DNI. When extended, the Concealability Rating is increased by 2.

*Gas-vent System	[Barrel Mount]*

*Gas-vent System*		(Rating 1)						200¥	Licence Restricted

*Improved Gas-vent System*	(Rating 2)						400¥ 	Licence Restricted

*Expert Gas-vent System*		(Rating 3)						600¥	Licence Restricted

Gas-vent recoil compression systems are barrel-mounted accessories that vent a weapon’s barrel gases at a specific vector to counter muzzle climb. Once installed, a gas-vent cannot be removed. Gas-vent systems provide a number of points of Recoil Compensation equal to their rating.

*Guncam		[Top, Under, Barrel, Side, Internal Mount]				Legal*

*Guncam*			(Rating 1)						350¥	Licence Restricted

*Guncam*			(Rating 2)						500¥ 	Licence Restricted

*Guncam*			(Rating 3)						650¥	Licence Restricted

The device that launched a thousand stupid-ass MeFeed videos. Whatever the gun is pointing at, it records. Yeah, you don’t always want a recording of what you’re about to shoot but sometimes that footage is invaluable – whether you need to show Mr. Johnson what you managed to pull off, review footage to help you plan your next move or doctor what you filmed to make you look good, the video you film has plenty of possible uses. Its Device Rating fills in for any necessary stats. Guncams can be installed in the Top, Under, Barrel, Side or Internal slots.

*Hidden Arm Slide	[Accessory]						600¥	Licence Restricted*

Attached to the forearm and worn under clothing, this slide can accommodate a hold-out, light pistol or taser. With a hand gesture, the slide releases the weapon right into your hand. If you quick draw the weapon in this slide, the threshold for a quick draw is 2. It also gives the weapon a -1 Concealability modifier. *Wireless*: You can ready the weapon in the slide as a Bonus Action.

*Holographic Sight	[Top Mount]						200¥	Legal*

Offers the same benefits as a laser sight without the red trail of light giving away the position of the shooter. In addition, the holographic (or holo) sight can display basic information such as range to target or remaining ammo without the wielder using AR. The only downside is the necessary top mount sometimes gets in the way, making quick draw attempts require 1 extra success.

*Holster, Concealable	[Accessory]						150¥	Legal*

This small holster can be worn on the ankle, clipped to the forearm, in the small of the back, or anywhere else it’s unlikely to be seen. The concealable holster adds -1 to the item’s Concealability. Only hold-outs, light pistols and tasers fit in a Concealable Holster.

*Holster, Quick-draw	[Accessory]						200¥	Legal*

This easy access holster can hold a weapon of light pistol or smaller size. It reduces the threshold for quick-drawing the holstered weapon by 1.

*Holster, Concealable Quick-draw	[Accessory]				500¥	Legal*

What more do you want a holster to do? You get to reduce the Concealability modifier of your weapon by 1 while the threshold to quick-draw a holstered weapon drops by 1. It won’t fire the thing for you though, so buckle down and do it yourself. Only hold-outs, light pistols and tasers fit in a Concealable Quick-draw Holster.

*Imaging Scope		[Top Mount]						300¥	Legal*

These classic scopes are attached to the top mount; attaching or removing them takes only a Simple Action. Imaging scopes include a micro camera and vision magnification and they have a Capacity of 3 to hold vision enhancements. *Wireless*: The scope’s vision can be shared, allowing you to share what your scope sees with your team (and yourself if you’re using it to look around a corner).

*Laser Sight		[Top or Under-barrel Mount]				125¥	Legal*

This device uses a laser beam to project a visible dot (in your choice of colours) on the target. This increases the weapon’s Accuracy by 1, which is not cumulative with smartlink modifiers. The laser sight can be attached to either the underbarrel mount or top mount. Activating or deactivating a laser sight is a Use Device Action.

*Longbarrel		[Barrel Mount]						300¥	Licence Restricted*

This modification involves replacing the stock barrel with a longer one thereby increasing bullet velocity. Increase Accuracy by 1, while increasing the Concealability modifier by +1.

*Retractable Bayonet	[Under-barrel Mount]					200¥	Legal*

This modification adds an underbarrel sheath that conceals a retractable bayonet. The bayonet can be extended as a Use Device Action. When attached to a Longarms weapon and extended, it has Reach 2, DV (STR+1)P and AP -1. If attached to a Pistol, the Reach is 1.

*Sawed Off/Shortbarrel	[Barrel Mount]						20¥	Licence Restricted*

This common modification reduced damage by 1 but increases Concealability by 1. It eliminates the gun’s ability to mount barrel modifications. If combined with stock removal, the Accuracy is also reduced by 1 in addition to the other benefits and penalties listed. Can only be used on Heavy Pistols and weapons in the Longarms skill group.

*Silencer/Suppressor	[Barrel Mount]						500¥	Forbidden Legality*

This barrel-mounted accessory reduces the sound and flash of a weapon’s discharge. It cannot be used with revolvers or shotguns. It applies a -4 dice pool modifier on all Perception Tests to notice the weapon’s use or locate the weapon’s firer. Attaching or removing a silencer takes a Complex Action.

*Shock Pad		[Stock Mount]						50¥	Legal*

A shock-absorbing pad is situated on the rigid stock of a rifle, shotgun or heavy weapon and provides 1 point of recoil compensation.

*Speed Loader		[Accessory]						25¥	Legal*

The speed loader is a simple device that holds a ring of bullets for fast insertion into a revolver’s cylinder. Each speed loader is specific to the weapon it was designed for. It lets you fully reload a revolver as a Complex Action instead of having to load rounds one at a time, loading only (Agility) rounds as a Complex Action.

*Stock Removal		[Stock Mount]						20¥	Legal*

Removing the stock reduces both the recoil compensation and the Concealability of a gun by 1. Weapon modifications such as a shock pad or any other stock modifications cannot be applied. If combined with sawed off the Accuracy is also reduced by 1 in addition to the other benefits and penalties listed.

*Trigger Removal								50¥	Legal*

Sometimes the time it takes to move a finger is too long. Sometimes the pressure of squeezing a trigger is enough to throw off the precision of a long range shot. This is the modification for those times. A smartgun system is necessary for trigger removal, singe the gun requires a command delivered wirelessly or through an optical cable to fire. This modification adds +1 Accuracy but is not cumulative with any other modification that adds to Accuracy other than the requisite smartlink. Wireless triggering requires wireless to be turned on. In case you were wondering.
#### **Sidebar: Quick Draw**
A character may attempt to quick-draw a pistol, pistol-sized weapon or small throwing weapon and immediately fire it by using a Quick Draw Simple Action. For a character to successfully draw the weapon, the player must make a (Weapon Skill) + Reaction [Physical] (3) Test. If the test is successful, the character draws the weapon and fires as a single Simple Action. If the test fails, the weapon is drawn but cannot be fired with the same action. If there is a glitch, the weapon is stuck in the holster or dropped and no more actions are allowed. In a critical glitch, a drawn blade may be fumbled out of the character’s reach or a pistol accidentally fired while still in the holster; the gamemaster decides the exact nature of the screw-up. Two weapons may be quick-drawn and fired simultaneously, but the dice pool is split and off-hand penalties apply.
### **Grenades**
Grenades are small, self-contained explosive packages. Use the Throwing Weapons skill when throwing grenades or Heavy Weapons when launching a grenade from a grenade launcher.

*Flash-bang	DV 10S AP-4							100¥	Licence Restricted*

Upon detonation, these “concussion” or “stun” grenades explode to create a bright, loud, shocking blast distributed equally over a radius of 10 metres.

*Gas								Chemical Cost+	40¥	Licence Restricted*

Instead of exploding, the gas grenade releases a cloud of gas over an area with a radius of 10 metres. This is usually riot control/CS gas, but many other chemical or toxin payloads can be chosen. The cloud lasts for approximately 10 Combat Turns (less in windy areas, longer in confined areas with poor ventilation).

*Smoke										40¥	Licence Restricted*

A smoke grenade releases a cloud of smoke over an areas with a diameter of 10 metres. The cloud obscures vision, applying visibility modifiers for smoke to relevant tests. The cloud lasts for approximately 10 Combat Turns (less in windy areas, longer in confined areas with poor ventilation). Heavy Smoke -6, Moderate Smoke -3, Light Smoke -1.

*Thermal Smoke									60¥	Licence Restricted*

A thermal smoke grenade contains hot particles designed to obscure thermographic vision. Once released, a cloud of smoke obscures an area with a diameter of 10 metres. The cloud obscures vision, applying visibility modifiers for thermal smoke to relevant tests. The cloud lasts for approximately 10 Combat Turns (less in windy areas, longer in confined areas with poor ventilation). Heavy Smoke -6, Moderate Smoke -3, Light Smoke -1.
### **Misc Equipment**

*Bug Scanner, Handheld									Licence Restricted*

*Rating 1										100¥*

*Rating 2										200¥*

*Rating 3										300¥*

Also called a radio signal scanner, this device locates and locks in wireless devices within 20 metres. The scanner can also measure a signal’s strength and pinpoint its location. To operate a bug scanner, roll Electronic Warfare + Logic [Rating]. A device that is running silent can use its Firewall [Firewall] to defend against the scan. If you get any net hits at all, you find the device. You may substitute the scanner’s Rating for your Electronic Warfare skill when you use it.

*Cyberware Scanner, Handheld								Licence Restricted*

*Rating 1										100¥*

*Rating 2										200¥*

*Rating 3										300¥*

Cyberware scanners, also known as millimetre wave detection systems, process video taken in the millimetre wave spectrum to identify the energy signature of cyberware and concealed items (specifically weapons) on a person. These devices can “see through” thick layers of clothing and other concealment to identify items from a distance of up to fifteen metres away. To determine if the detector scans cyberware or a prohibited item, roll twice the Rating of the scanner (and any dice pool modifier from the table below) and compare the hits scored to the thresholds given on the Cyberware Scanner Table. Millimetre wave scans can detect any non-biological item by its shape and composition, assuming the item is listed in the device’s database. If the threshold is reached, the scanner detects the item/implant and notes its general locations and type; additional hits provide more detail (function, model, grade, etc.).

|**Cyberware Scanner Table**||
| :- | :- |
|**|Item**|**Threshold**|
|Standard cyberware, weapons|1|
|Alphaware, other items|2|
|Betaware|3|
|Deltaware|5+|
|**Situation**|**Modifier**|
|2 or more implants/items|+1|
|4 or more implants/items|+2|
|6 or more implants/items|+3|

*MCT Cyberscanner Ring								Licence Restricted*

*Rating 2									240¥*

This ring allows for more subtle scanning for cyberware.

*Data Tap									300¥	Licence Restricted*

You use this hacking tool by attaching it to a data cable. Once it’s clamped onto the cable, you can use it via universal data connector. Any device directly connected to the data tap also has a direct connection with the devices on either end of the cable and vice versa. The tap can be removed without damaging the cable. The data-tap can be wirelessly commanded to self-destruct as a Bonus Action, immediately and instantly severing the direct connection. This does not harm the cable.

*Duct Tape, roll									5¥	Legal*

Known for its versatility, ubiquitousness and downright usefulness, duct tape is a plastic adhesive tape, usually black, grey or silver in colour whose usefulness is apparent to anybody who’s ever had a breakage of any kind that has to be temporarily held together.

*Fire Blanket									10¥	Legal*

This 1m x 1m fire blanket is made using fibre drill fabric, a specially treated glass fibre that is smooth, soft and dense, ensuring no irritation to the skin. It offers superior protection for both people and objects that need safeguarding from intense heat. You gain a +2 dice pool bonus when it is used to extinguish a fire. The standard test to put out a fire with a fire blanket is a Agility + Intuition Test, reducing the fire’s DV by 1 for each hit.

*Fire Extinguisher, Portable*

*CO2		(0.5 kgs)								100¥	Legal*

*Dry Powder	(0.5 kgs)								25¥	Legal*

*Wet Chemical	(0.5 kgs)								50¥	Legal*

Sometimes things just catch on fire. It’s not *always* a shadowrunner’s fault. But this way you can at least put the fire out before your gear goes up in flames. You gain a +12 dice pool bonus when it is used to extinguish a fire. The standard test to put out a fire with a fire blanket is a Agility + Intuition Test, reducing the fire’s DV by 1 for each hit.

*Flashlight*

*Standard Flashlight								25¥	Legal*

*Low-Light Flashlight								25¥	Legal*

*Thermographic Flashlight								25¥	Legal*

By 2075, most flashlights are long lasting and super bright. Durability and brightness depend on the size – the bulkier, the better. Flashlights are also available in low-light and infrared versions, reducing visibility modifiers for low-light and thermographic vision, respectively. A flashlight can also be mounted to a weapon’s top or under-barrel mount.

*Geiger Counter										Legal*

*Rating 1										100¥*

*Rating 2										200¥*

*Rating 3										300¥*

This sensor picks up the amount of radioactivity surrounding it.

*Radiation Vibration Earring							Legal*

*Rating 2							240¥*

This earring vibrates at a frequency that changes depending on the level of radiation detected.

*Light Stick									5¥	Legal*

Bend, snap and shake it for a couple of hours of chemical light.

*Magnesium Torch								25¥	Legal*

Strike and activate for five minutes of bright torchlight.

*Rappelling Gloves								50¥	Legal*

These gloves are made of a special fabric that allows the wearer to get a tighter grip on a grapple line, giving them a +2 dice pool bonus on all tests to hold their grip on the line. These gloves are necessary in order to use ultrathin microwire.

*Restraints*							

*Disposable Plastic Straps (10 pk)	(Armour 6, Structure 1)			5¥	Legal*

*Metal					(Armour 16, Structure 2)		20¥	Legal*

*Plasteel					(Armour 20, Structure 2)		50¥	Licence Restricted*

*Containment Manacles			(Armour 16, Structure 2)		250¥	Licence Restricted*

Disposable plastic straps are lightweight and easy to carry in bundles. Standard metal restraints come with a mechanical or a wireless-controlled lock. Modern plasteel restraints are flash-fused and remain in place until the subject is cut free. Containment manacles are metal and attached to a prisoner’s wrists or ankles to prevent them from moving faster than a shuffle or extending a cyber-implant weapon.

*Diving Gear									2,000¥	Legal*

Underwater diving equipment, including a diving suit, partial facemask with snorkel, breathing regulator, an air tank with 2 hours of air and in inflatable vest for quick returns to the surface. The regulator and air tank protect against inhalation toxins just like a gas mask. The wet suit provides Rating 1 resistance to Cold Damage. Wireless signals don’t work very well underwater but the wireless systems in the diving gear help with prep and maintenance.
### **Bags**

*Small Pouch									5¥	Legal*

### **Audio Enhancement**
Non-cyberware enhancements for equipment. Each enhancement has an associated Capacity cost.

*Audio Enhancement									Legal*

*Rating 1									1 Cap	500¥*

*Rating 2									2 Cap 	1,000¥*

*Rating 3									3 Cap 	1,500¥*

Audio enhancement allows the user to hear a broader spectrum of audio frequencies, including high and low frequencies outside the normal metahuman audible spectrum. The user also experiences fine discrimination of nuances and can block out distracting background noise. Audio enhancement adds its Rating as a dice pool bonus and Limit.

*Sound Filter										Legal*

*Rating 1									1 Cap	250¥*	

*Rating 2									2 Cap	500¥*

*Rating 3									3 Cap	750¥*

This lets you block out background noise and focus on specific sounds or patterns of sounds. It even includes speech, word and sound pattern recognition. Each Rating point lets you select a single sound group (such as the footsteps of a patrolling guard or the rotors of a distant helicopter) and focus on it. You only actively listen to one group at a time, but you can record the others for later playback or set them to triggered monitoring (such as sounding an alert if a conversation brings up a certain topic or if there’s a variation in the breathing pattern of a guard dog).

*Spatial Recogniser							2 Cap	1,000¥	Legal*

This hearing accessory pinpoints the source of a sound. You get a +2 dice pool bonus to your audio-based Perception Tests and their limit.

### **Headgear**

*Gas Mask									200¥	Legal*

This air-supplied re-breather completely covers your face and gives you immunity to inhalation-vector toxin attacks. It comes with a one-hour clean-air supply (replacements cost 40¥) and can be attached to larger air tanks. It cannot be combined with a regular respirator. With a wireless connection or a data filament connection, the gas mask analyses and gives you information about the surrounding air that you’re *not* breathing.

*Respirator										Legal*

A respirator is a filter-mask worn over the mouth and nose that protects against inhalation-vector toxins. The respirator adds a rating (listed below) to toxin resistance tests against inhalation-vector toxins.

*Cheap Respirator		+2 dice pool bonus						100¥*

*Good Respirator		+4 dice pool bonus						200¥*

*Excellent Respirator	+6 dice pool bonus						300¥*

*Smart Wig									1,200¥	Legal*

Designed for fashion, but immensely useful for clandestine operations. This wig can change colour, curl or straighten, lengthen or shorten and shift to a number of preprogrammed hairstyles on command. The wig can transform to any of four saved styles as a Standard Action.

With a wireless connection the wig can transform to any style which can be downloaded from any of several Matrix databases offering basic styles for free and styles worn by famous people offered at premium prices.

You can also design your own styles with a Software + Logic [Mental] Test and use them yourself or post them online.

*Smart Wig with Trode Rig							1,300¥	Legal*

A built-in trode net is an optional extra for the smart wig, allowing a direct neural interface (DNI).

*Synthskin Face Mask							100¥/Rating	Forbidden Legality*

The synthskin facemask is composed of a programmable electropolymer commonly used in the skin covering of synthetic cyberware and humanoid mimic drones. It produces a lifelike replica of an individual’s face. A person’s face can be duplicated if you have a scan from a biometric reader (with a dice pool bonus on the Disguise Test equal to the biometric reader’s Rating). A Software + Logic Test (with a dice pool bonus on the Disguise Test equal to the successes) can replicate a specific individual’s face or create a completely unique appearance. In either case, the limit on the test is equal to the Rating of the mask. The mask is reusable in the sense that it can be worn multiple times, but once an appearance has been set in either fashion described above, it cannot be altered.

*Trodes									2 Cap	70¥	Legal*

Available as a headband, net or full-on cap, the electrode-and-ultrasound net gives you a direct neural interface. Useful if you’re too squeamish to get a hold drilled in your head for a datajack.
