### **Vision Enhancement**
Non-cyberware enhancements for equipment. A number of options are available for installation in visual sensors and imaging devices from contacts to cameras. Each enhancement has an associated Capacity cost.

*Flare Compensation							1 Cap		250¥	Legal*

This protects you from blinding flashes of light as well as simple glare. It mitigates the vision modifiers for glares and reduces the penalty from flashing lights.

*Image Link								1 Cap		25¥	Legal*

A standard upgrade, this lets you display visual information (text, pictures, movies, the current time, etc.) in your field of vision. This is usually AROs, but you can display pretty much whatever you want to on it. You and your team can use it to share tactical and situational info in real time. An image link is what you need to truly “see” AR and participate in the modern world.

*Low-Light Vision							1 Cap		500¥	Legal*

This allows you to see normally in light levels as low as starlight. It doesn’t help in total darkness, though.

*Polychromic Lens (Contacts only)					1 Cap		100¥	Legal*

This feature can be added to contacts and allows an individual to change the apparent colour and pattern of their retina. The contacts can be changed via wireless connection to any appearance imaginable, though the resolution is not as precise as Retinal Duplication cyberware and cannot fool a biometric reader.

*Smartlink								1 Cap		2,000¥	Restricted Licence*

This accessory interacts with a smartgun system to project the weapon’s angle of fire into the user’s vision, centring red crosshairs where the user is pointing and highlighting perceived targets. The smartgun’s laser rangefinder also calculates and displays the distance to the target. Additional data from the weapon, such as the ammunition level, heat buildup and stress can also be displayed. Requires an Image Link.

*Thermographic Vision							1 Cap		500¥	Legal*

This enables vision in the infrared spectrum, enabling you to see heat patterns. It’s a very practical way to spot living beings in areas of total darkness, to check if a motor or machine has been running lately and so on.

*Vision Enhancement										Legal*

*Rating 1									1 Cap		500¥*

*Rating 2									1 Cap		1,000¥*

*Rating 3									1 Cap		1,500¥*

This sharpens a character’s vision at all ranges, providing visual acuity closer to that of the average hawk than that of the average metahuman. It adds its Rating as a dice pool modifier to your visual Perception Tests and their Limit.

*Vision Magnification							1 Cap		250¥	Legal*

This zoom function digitally magnifies vision up to fifty times, allowing distant targets to be seen clearly. After using a Take Aim action, you reduce the Range modifier by one category.
### **Electronic Accessories**

*AR Gloves	(Device Rating 3)							150¥	Legal*

AR gloves allow you to manually interact with the Matrix in Augmented Reality mode, letting you “touch” and “hold” virtual AROs and receiving tactile force-feedback.

*Meta AR Gloves (Device Rating 1)				50¥	Legal*

Plain grey gloves in a “one-size-fits-all” size that allow AR manipulation.

*AR Nails		(Device Rating 1)						200¥	Legal*

Synthetic fingernails that function the same as AR gloves.

*Biometric Reader	(Device Rating 3)						200¥	Legal*

Sometimes someone online likes to know it’s really you. This handheld device can be used for fingerprints, retina scans, voice patterns, tongue prints – pretty much anything but a DNA scan. You can use it to lock your electronics so only you (or one of your body parts) can unlock it.

*Datachip										5¥	Legal*

For occasions when you want to transfer data by physical means – like bringing the project specs on the competition’s new cyberdeck to Mr Johnson in person at the meet – a datachip can hold enormous quantities of data in a small finger-sized chip, accessible to any electronic device. Datachips have no wireless capability, so you need to plug them into a universal data connector (found on any device) if you want to read or write to them.

*Electronic Paper	(Device Rating 1)						5¥	Legal*

This electronic sheet is anywhere from post-it note to poster sized and it can be folded or rolled up. It digitally displays images, text, data or video and can act as a touchscreen. Electronic paper is wireless and can be written on or erased wirelessly. Sometimes hacker gangs cover the surfaces of buildings in electronic paper so they are constantly changing and overwritten with graffiti that can be seen even by people with their AR image-links turned off.

*Hitcher Jack										250¥	Legal*

This cyberdeck attachment allows non-cybered companions to accompany a decker into the Matrix. They can view the Matrix as the decker views it but cannot interact with it.

*RFID												Legal*

These tiny computers (named after old-fashioned radio frequency identification tags) form an integral part of every product commercially available in the Sixth World. Ranging in size from microscopic to slightly larger than a price tag, RFID tags have a stick-to-anything adhesive backing and can be tricky to spot. Tags are used for geo-tagging locations and objects, leaving a virtual AR message for anyone who comes by, employee tracking, access control, owner-contact information for everything from vehicles to pets, vehicle and weapon registration and so on. They can also be used as tracking devices, periodically transmitting GPS data to the Matrix.

`	`*Security Tags							10¥	Legal*

Security-conscious megacorps often implant these security tags in their sararimen and valued citizens, either to monitor employee workplace productivity, grant and deny clearance and security access or track employees in the case of abduction or extraction (or escape). These same tags are used on incarcerated and paroled criminals and parents and schools also use them to track students. Security tags cannot be simply erased with a tag eraser due to EMP hardening. If a tag is implanted under the skin, an Extended Medicine + Logic [Mental] (10, 1 minute) Test is needed to remove it.

`	`*Sensor Tags							40¥	Legal*

A sensor RFID can be equipped with a single sensor (sold separately) of up to Rating 2. It then records everything it can, to a maximum of 24 hours of time, at which point it can be programmed to either shut off or overwrite data older than 24 hours. Sensor tags are often used for diagnostic purposes in various devices.

*Stealth Tags							20¥	License Restricted*

A stealth tag always runs in hidden mode and usually has a Stealth Rating equal to its Device Rating. Stealth tags are often used as backup for security tags by megacorps that are security conscious (and sneaky). They can be implanted the same way security tags can.

*Simrig			(Device Rating 3)						1,000¥	Legal*

This simsense recorder can record experience data (sensory and emotive) from you or whoever is wearing it. Simrigs are used to make the most of the simsense chips sold on the market. You’ll need to have a working sim module (with the DNI interface) to make a recording.

*Subvocal Microphone	(Device Rating 1)						50¥	Legal*

The next best thing to telepathy is the ability to stage-whisper at any range. Attached with adhesive to your throat, this hard-to-spot microphone lets you communicate via subvocalized speech. A -4 dice pool modifier is applied to Perception Tests to overhear you when you’re subvocalizing.

*Tag Eraser										450¥	Licence Restricted*

This handheld device creates a strong electromagnetic field perfect for burning out RFID tags and other small, unshielded electronics. When you bring the eraser within 5 millimetres of an electronic device and activate it, the device takes 10 boxes of Matrix damage (resisted normally). The tag eraser has one charge but can be full recharged at a power point in 10 seconds.

*Trid Projector		(Device Rating 3)						200¥	Legal*

This device projects a trideo hologram into a five-meter cube right next to or above the device. The hologram can be quite realistic, but unless you’re really artistic about it, it’s pretty obvious that it’s just trid.

*White Noise Generator										Legal*

*Rating 1											50¥*

*Rating 2											100¥*

*Rating 3											150¥*

*Rating 4											200¥*

*Rating 5											250¥*

*Rating 6											300¥*

This device creates a field of random noise, masking the sounds within its area and preventing direct audio surveillance. All Perception Tests to overhear a conversation within (Rating) meters of a white noise generator receive a dice pool penalty equal to twice the device’s Rating. If more than one generator is in use, only count the highest rating. A white noise generator is redundant in a noisy environment (such as a nightclub or a firefight) and does not help to curtail video surveillance or jam wireless signals.
### **Biotech**

*Medkit (Rating 1-6)*

|**Rating**|**Example Contents**|**Conceal Mod**|**Cost**|
| :- | :- | :- | :- |
|**1**|Bandages, tape, scissors, iodine irrigation, oral pain meds and nausea meds. Expert System: basic medication database, anatomy tutorial, disease wiki|Large Pocket (-2)|100¥|
|**2**|As above plus splints, disposable syringes, selection of IV drugs for push, antibiotics, flashlight, trauma sheers. Expert System: basic disease summaries, extensive medication database|Small pouch or fanny pack (-1)|400¥|
|**3**|As above plus airway supplies, IV tubing, selection of IV drugs for infusion, oxygen mask, thermal blanket. Expert System: simple diagnostic algorithms, clinical calculators, detailed disease summaries|Large Pouch or fanny pack (+0)|900¥|
|**4**|As above plus basic surgical tools, selection of slap patches or autoinjector. Expert System: advanced diagnostic algorithms, guide to simple procedures|Small backpack or duffel bag (+1)|1600¥|
|**5**|As above plus injectable treatments, StatScan hand-held imager. Expert System: online Matrix support, guide to advanced procedures|Large backpack or duffel bag (+2)|2500¥|
|**6**|As above plus full surgical tools, sterile drapes, anaesthetic gases. Expert System: expert Matrix support, step-by-step guide to simple surgeries|Oversized duffel bag or larger (+3)|3600¥|

The medkit includes medical supplies, bandages, tools, and a (talkative) doctor expert system that can advise the user on techniques to handle most typical medical emergencies (including fractures, gunshot wounds, chemical wounds and poisoning, as well as offering advice for the treating of shock, handling blood loss, and of course performing resuscitations). Add the medkit’s rating to your dice pool on First Aid tests. The medkit needs to be restocked after every (Rating uses).

*Biomonitor										300¥	Legal*

This compact device measures life signs – heart rate, blood pressure, temperature and so on. The biomonitor can also analyse blood, sweat and skin samples. Used by medical services and patients who need to monitor their own health, biomonitors can be worn as an armband or wristband or integrated into clothing or commlinks. Attaching a biomonitor is a Simple Action.
#### **Slap Patches**
Slap patches are adhesive dermal chemical dispensers that allow continual, safe administration of chemicals. They are applied directly to the patient’s skin. Applying a slap patch to an unwilling patient’s requires a successful melee attack (which deals no damage), which may be tricky if the target doesn’t have much exposed skin. Applying a slap patch is a Simple Action.

*Stim Patch											Legal*

*Rating 1											25¥*

*Rating 2											50¥*

*Rating 3											750¥*

*Rating 4											100¥*

*Rating 5											125¥*

*Rating 6											150¥*

This patch removes a number of boxes of Stun damage equal to its Rating. This effect lasts for (Rating x 10) minutes – after that period of time the patient takes (Rating +1) unresisted Stun damage (which may become physical overflow by that point). While the stimulant patch is in effect, the character is unable to rest. Frequent use of stimulant patches may require Addiction Tests. Treat it as Addiction Rating 2, Addiction Threshold 1.

*Trauma Patch										500¥	Legal*

If placed on a dying patient, this allows them to make an immediate stabilisation test using Body + Willpower (3). If successful, the wounded patient stabilises and no longer takes automatic additional damage. Additional stabilisation tests can be made, at a cumulative -2 dice pool modifier per test.

*Tranq Patch (Rating 1-10)	Rating x 20¥*

This patch inflicts Stun damage equal to its rating, resisted with Body.

*Vasotech Autoinjection Gun									Legal*

The Vasotech Multidose Autoinjector System is a favourite among military and civilian combat medics. These compact handheld devices resemble a pistol. When pressed against a subject’s skin, the autoinjector rapidly sterilised a small field and administers an injection from a multidose drug reservoir. The MD-9 model features a single larger reservoir that stores up to nine doses, whereas the newer MD-3X model features three smaller reservoirs, each of which holds up to three doses. In game terms, an autoinjector allows a medic to administer an injectable drug with a Simple Action. Changing reservoirs with the MD-3X requires a Use Device Action.

*MD-9 Autoinjection Gun								1,000¥*

*MD-3X Autoinjection Gun								1,500¥*
### **Drugs**

*Aztech Chew									10¥	Legal*

Vector: Ingestion, Inhalation

Speed: 1 minute

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: Physiological & Psychological [Rating 2 (2)]

Effect: +1 Reaction, Pain Resistance 1

This legal drug first gained popularity in the early days of the Native American Nations and is traditionally made from an ancient formula including tobacco leaves, cannabis resin and willow bark. Modern aztech chew typically forgoes the expensive natural ingredients by directly combining the active chemical compounds involved: THC, nicotine and salicin. Aztech chew users claim the drug has a calming effect. Once the effect wears off, users experience -1 Intuition for a time period equivalent to twice the original duration. Some claim that long-term users are more susceptible to fatigue and cancer.

*Betel										5¥	Legal*

Vector: Ingestion

Speed: Immediate

Duration: 10 x 1D6 minutes

Addiction Type: Physiological [Special]

Effect: +1 Perception

An ancient and widespread Asian practice of chewing nuts and leaves of the betel tree with lime has led to the synthesis of Wuxing’s highly addictive and legal betel chewing gum. Betel is a mild stimulant with cavity-fighting properties; users commonly feel awake and alert when using it. Rather than making an Addiction Test, characters who use betel, even once, gain a Mild addiction to it. A character may never have an addiction worse than Mild to betel. Characters who add dice to toxin resistance tests are immune to this effect if they succeed at a Toxin Resistance Test. Because it is instantly addictive, betel often serves as a gateway drug to more powerful stimulants.

*Bliss										30¥	Forbidden Legality*

Vector: Inhalation, Injection

Speed: 1 Combat Turn

Duration: (6-Body) hours, minimum 1 hour

Addiction Type: Physiological & Psychological [Rating 5 (3)]

Effect: -1 Reaction, +1 to all thresholds, -1 to all Limits, High Pain Tolerance 3

A tranquilising narcotic, bliss is an opiate synthesised from poppy plants. It takes its name from the sensations its users feel.

*Brass Balls									60¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: Immediate

Duration: (12-Body) hours, minimum 1 hour

Addiction Type: Physiological & Psychological [Rating 5 (3)]

Effect: Immunity to Fear (see below)

This drug suppresses the functions of the brain that govern fear, both innate and learned. For the duration of the drug’s effects, the character is immune to fear (including negative results from Composure Tests) and fear-based powers/attacks. As a drawback, however, the character becomes reckless, incautious and also less inhibited. At the gamemaster’s discretion, they may call for the character to make a Logic + Willpower (3) Test to avoid doing something that would normally be considered foolish, dangerous or socially inappropriate.

*Cram										20¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Ingestion, Inhalation

Speed: 10 minutes

Duration: (12-Body) hours, minimum 1 hour

Addiction Type: Psychological [Rating 4 (3)]

Effect: +1 Reaction, +1D6 Initiative Dice

Cram is an extremely popular stimulant. When this drug wears off, users crash and suffer 6 Stun damage (unresisted). Cram users appear hyper-alert, almost to the point of paranoia. They react quickly, often without thought and they’re prone to irrational outbursts. Other common side effects are jitteriness and fidgeting.

*Crash										800¥	Legal*

Vector: Injection

Speed: Immediate

Power: Special

Addiction Type: None

Effect: Special

Crash is an injectable form of the potent vasoactive and stimulant drugs found in a trauma patch. When given intravenously, crash allows the subject to make a Stabilisation Test using Body + Willpower (3). If successful, the wounded patient stabilises and no longer takes automatic additional damage. Additional stabilisation tests can be made, at a cumulative -2 dice pool modifier per test.

*Jazz										75¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: Immediate

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: Physiological & Psychological [Rating 8 (3)]

Effect: +1 Reaction, +1 Physical Limit, +2D6 Initiative Dice

Jazz is a stimulant designed to better the odds for run-of-the-mill law-enforcement officers who run up against augmented street samurai. It’s usually taken from a single-dose inhaler (or “popper”) When jazz wears off, the user crashes and is flooded with despondent and miserable emotions, suffering the effects of Disorientation for a duration equal to the duration of the initial effects. While cram makes people hyper and twitchy, jazz makes people as jumpy and hyper as caffeinated two-year-olds.

*Kamikaze									100¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: Immediate

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: Physiological [Rating 9 (3)]

Effect: +1 Body, +1 Agility, +2 Strength, +1 Willpower, +2 Physical Limit, +2D6 Initiative Dice, High Pain Tolerance 3

Kamikaze is a tailored combat stimulant. When kamikaze wears off, the user crashes and suffers -1 Reaction, -1 Willpower and -2 to all Limits for a duration equal to that of the initial effect. They also suffer 6 Stun damage (unresisted). The repeated use of kamikaze has a destructive effect on the user’s metabolism. Large doses can cause excitement, tremors, momentary euphoria and dilated pupils. Excess doses (bordering on overdose level) cause anxiety, hallucinations and uncontrolled muscular movements. Even higher dosages lead to death. Kamikaze users are near-crazed, filled with a feeling of imperviousness and invincibility, exhibiting almost no regard for their own well-being. They can be entertaining to watch, as long as you’re not in front of them.

*Long Haul									50¥	Legal*

Vector: Injection

Speed: 10 minutes

Duration: 4 days

Addiction Type: Psychological [Rating 2 (1)]

Effect: Alleviates need for sleep

A combination of synthesised hormones and other brain-regulating chemicals, long haul stimulates the brain and keeps the user awake, obviating the need for sleep. A character dosed on long haul can remain awake for four days – without incurring any modifiers from fatigue or weariness. After this time, however, the user immediately passes out and sleeps soundly for 8D6 hours. If the character is kept awake during this period, he suffers from disorientation as he is afflicted with hallucinations and an inability to concentrate. If a second dose of long haul is taken after the first has worn off, the character can stay awake an additional 1D6 /2 days. After that period, they suffer 10 Stun damage (unresisted) and must crash as detailed above. Long haul cannot keep a character awake past this point, no matter how many additional doses are administered.

*Nitro										50¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: 1 Combat Turn

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: Physiological & Psychological [Rating 9 (3)]

Effect: +2 Strength, +2 Willpower, +2 Perception, +2 Physical Limit, High Pain Tolerance 6

A dangerous combination of potent drugs favoured by troll gangers, nitro is a powerful stimulant that can easily kill a user. After the drug’s effects wear off, the subject suffers -2 to all limits and takes 9 Stun damage (unresisted) for an equal duration. Nitro users feel infused with energy, suffer a diminished attention span and talk incessantly (even to themselves).

*Ondansetron									50¥	Legal*

Vector: Ingestion, Injection

Speed: Immediate

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: None

Effect: Counteracts the effects of Nausea

Ondansetron is a powerful anti-emetic drug that works rapidly on the central nervous system to relieve nausea. When administered to a character suffering from the effects of Nausea, double the subject’s Willpower for the purposes of determining incapacitation. Ondansetron also halves the duration of Nausea.

*Zen										50¥	Restricted Licence*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: 5 minutes

Duration: 10 x 1d6 minutes

Addiction Type: Psychological [Rating 3 (1)]

Effect: -2 Reaction, +1 Willpower, -1 physical action dice pool penalty

A psychedelic hallucinogen, zen is popular among those looking to escape reality or seeking trance-like states.
### **Toxins**
Knockout drugs. Truth serum. Nerve gas. All of these are examples of toxins, a catch-all term for a substance that’s mostly meant for use as a weapon, as opposed to recreation. Each substance has several attribute ratings.

*CS/Tear Gas									20¥	Restricted Legality*

Vector: Contact, Inhalation

Speed: 1 Combat Turn

Penetration: 0

Power: 8

Effect: Disorientation, Nausea, Stun Damage

CS gas is an irritant that affects the eyes, skin and mucus membranes, causing them to burn to water. It also stimulates a physiological panic response: increased heart rate, shortness of breath and so forth. Washing thoroughly with soap and water can remove CS from the victim’s skin, thus ending the duration of the nausea prematurely. CS gas becomes inert after two minutes of contact with the air.

*Narcoject									50¥	Restricted Legality*

Vector: Injection

Speed: Immediate

Penetration: 0

Power: 15

Effect: Stun Damage

A common tranquiliser, narcoject is typically used with dart guns. It has no side effects.

*Nausea Gas									25¥	Restricted Legality*

Vector: Inhalation

Speed: 3 Combat Turns

Penetration: 0

Power: 9

Effect: Disorientation, Nausea

Used as a riot control agent, this gas causes nausea and a crippling need to vomit. Nausea gas becomes inert after two minutes of contact with the air.

*Pepper Punch									5¥	Legal*

Vector: Contact, Inhalation

Speed: 1 Combat Turn

Penetration: 0

Power: 11

Effect: Nausea, Stun Damage

Pepper punch is an irritant combining CS and oleo-capsicum, the active ingredient in hot peppers, along with other chemicals. It is typically deployed as a liquid spray for personal defence and deterrence; this agent is often tagged with RFID tags or special dyes to identify victims later. Someone dosed with pepper punch feels an intense burning on any affected skin; this effect is even more pronounced if it gets in the eyes, nose or mouth. Victims sprayed in the eyes have trouble seeing and breathing becomes difficult.


**<a name="_toc218024815"></a>SPECIALIST GEAR**\

===============================================
### **Cyberdecks**
If you were a decker and someone swung a monofilament claymore at you, you’d protect your cyberdeck with your body and not the other way around. This isn’t just because the things are fraggin’ expensive – cyberdecks (or decks) are a decker’s life’s blood, an all-in-one ticket to hacking the planet. The most common form of a deck is a smooth, flat, elongated rectangle, slim with plenty of display space for touch controls, although they can take many forms.

All cyberdecks include illegal hot-sim modules right out of the box.

It can act like a commlink and has all the features of a commlink in addition to the cool hacking stuff.

*Radio Shack PCD-500						19,200¥			Licence Restricted*

*Response 1	Signal 1	Firewall 1	System 1		Processor Limit 2	Matrix Condition 7*

*Programs: Analyse 1, Browse 1, Command 1, Edit 1*

This little wonder is the perfect model for the aspiring young cybersecurity specialist. Bulk discount for educational institutions – contact a sales representative for details. Are you going to squeeze a lot of power out of it? No. But it’s like the Radio Shack motto says: “Radio Shack: Better than nothing, most of the time!”

*Little Hornet							38,400¥			Licence Restricted*

*Response 2	Signal 3	Firewall 1	System 2		Processor Limit 4	Matrix Condition 8*

*Programs: Analyse 2, Browse 2, Command 2, Edit 2*

This compact cyberdeck is made in Chicago under the UCAS ghoul employment program and we pass the savings right on to you! Its high end goes to pretty good heights but watch out for the low end.

*Hermes Chariot							79,500¥			Licence Restricted*

*Response 4	Signal 4	Firewall 3	System 3		Processor Limit 6	Matrix Condition 10*

*Programs: Analyse 2, Browse 3, Command 3, Edit 2*

This cyber-chariot allows deckers to ride out in confidence and style. At least, that’s what the advertising promises. In reality, it is an effective deck for the budget conscious managing small sites. Powerful enough to dump any script-kiddies who are playing in your turf, but lacking the power to battle master deckers, who probably wouldn’t be after data in the kind of system you’re guarding anyway.

*Novatech Navigator						119,200¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 5	Signal 4	Firewall 5	System 4		Processor Limit 8	Matrix Condition 10*

*Programs: Analyse 4, Browse 5, Command 3, Edit 4*

This cyberdeck was built with its purpose in mind. If offers speed, power and protection, while cutting down on areas more important to riggers that deckers, such as signal and command programs. The decker with a Novatech Navigator and true skill can navigate through hosts and slice ice with the big boys.

*Renraku Tsurugi						139,650¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 5	Signal 5	Firewall 5	System 5		Processor Limit 8	Matrix Condition 11*

*Programs: Analyse 5, Browse 5, Command 4, Edit 5*

While released as the better, faster, stronger competitor with the Novatech Navigator, this cyberdeck didn’t gain the market lead its creators hoped for. While critics acknowledge that it is overall a more powerful deck that many of its rivals, it also has a price that’s higher as well. The question raised by critics is whether all the features will be utilised by the typical user and, if not, whether it’s worth paying the premium for them?

*Shiawase Cyber-4						159,650¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 6	Signal 5	Firewall 5	System 5		Processor Limit 9	Matrix Condition 11*

*Programs: Analyse 4, Browse 5, Command 5, Edit 5*

The first product of Shiawase’s reboot of the Fuchi Cyber line, the Cyber-5, was a deck that had high praise but low sales figures, criticised for being out of reach of the larger cybersecurity market. The Cyber-4 was introduced as a low-price, high-performance cyberdeck, undercutting the price point of the CIY-720 while outperforming the more popular cyberdeck in some areas. This model will save you a lot of money but has its own flaws. Tread carefully. 

*XIAO MPG-1							172,650¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 6	Signal 6	Firewall 5	System 5		Processor Limit 10	Matrix Condition 12*

*Programs: Analyse 5, Browse 5, Command 4, Edit 5*

The MPG-1 is designed by our friends at the Midwest Pirate’s Guild with one deadly purpose: smash everything in your way before it can hit back. Lots of IC was harmed in the making of this deck.

*Sony CIY-720							173,100¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 5	Signal 6	Firewall 5	System 6		Processor Limit 10	Matrix Condition 12*

*Programs: Analyse 5, Browse 6, Command 4, Edit 6*

This cyberdeck filled a high-end niche at the time with strong performance and a price point midway between its competitors. However, with the almost simultaneous release of the Shiawase Cyber-4 just undercutting the price, sales dropped significantly below predictions. While the timing was suspicious, that’s the way of the free market.

*Global Sandstorm Sirocco					186,250¥		Licence Restricted*

*Response 6	Signal 5	Firewall 6	System 6		Processor Limit 10	Matrix Condition 13*

*Programs: Analyse 6, Browse 5, Command 5, Edit 5*

*Hardening: 1*

The Sirocco was based on designs by Sandstorm Engineering before the merger with Global Oil to form Global Sandstorm. It became the peak of security spider anti-decker tech in the middle east.
### **Control Rig**
This implant harnesses the raw data-co-ordinating and synchronisation power of the middle brain for the express purpose of directly manipulating rigged vehicles and drones (and other devices with rigger interface, like turrets). It has a built-in sim module, so you can use it for DNI with other devices. It also comes with a universal data connector and about a meter of retractable cable (it’s like getting a free datajack). When you’re jumped into a vehicle or drone, the control rig provides its Rating as a dice pool bonus on all Vehicle skill tests. Additionally, the rating of your control rig is added to the Handling and Acceleration of any vehicle you are jumped into. As if that was not enough, your Vehicle Test thresholds are reduced by the rating of your control rig (to a minimum of 1), even when you’re jumped in.

*Control Rig										Licence Restricted*

*Rating 1							0.5 Essence	10,000¥*

*Rating 2							1 Essence		25,000¥*
### **Rigger Command Console (RCC)**
A deck for controlling drones, vehicles and security systems. It’s about the size of a briefcase. The main purpose of the RCC is to create a PAN with your drones. If a drone is slaved to a rigger command console and isn’t running any of its own programs, it uses the programs running on the RCC. This can exceed its normal program limit.

It can act like a commlink and has all the features of a commlink in addition to the cool drone stuff.

*Rigger Command Console								Licence Restricted*

Rating 1		*Noise Reduction 1	Sharing 1*					1,400¥

Rating 2		*Noise Reduction 2	Sharing 2*					8,000¥

Rating 3		*Noise Reduction 3	Sharing 3*					16,000¥

Rating 4		*Noise Reduction 4	Sharing 4*					32,000¥

Rating 5		*Noise Reduction 5	Sharing 5*					64,000¥

### <a name="_hlk205134481"></a>**Matrix Programs**
Programs come in two categories. Common programs are <a name="_hlk205134492"></a>ones that are pretty harmless and available almost anywhere for hobbyists and Matrix professionals. Hacking programs are more dangerous and illegal to buy, own or use without a licence.

*Analyse Program							Legal*

Rating 2							100¥

Rating 3							150¥

Rating 4							300¥

Rating 5							450¥

Rating 6							600¥

Analyse programs gather data about icons and nodes in the Matrix by issuing queries, analysing system resources, performing registry lookups and so on.

*Browse Program							Legal*

Rating 2							100¥

Rating 3							150¥

Rating 4							300¥

Rating 5							450¥

Rating 6							600¥

Browse programs are specialised search routines that help track down information on a particular node or in the Matrix at large.

*Command Program							Legal*

Rating 2							100¥

Rating 3							150¥

Rating 4							300¥

Rating 5							450¥

Rating 6							600¥

Command programs give the user a modular and customisable control interface for various devices. The allows the user to control a device through the Matrix.

*Edit Program								Legal*

Rating 2							100¥

Rating 3							150¥

Rating 4							300¥

Rating 5							450¥

Rating 6							600¥

Edit is a combination word processor, graphic design tool and video/animation editor. You can use it to create and alter files of any media type: text, graphics, video, trideo, simsense, etc. Edit sees common usage in the corporate world but hackers use it for their own subversive ends.

*Armour Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Armour programs are software redundancy and automatic backup systems that protect personas from attacks that cause Matrix Damage.

*Attack Program								Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Attack programs are hostile code carriers that attempt to kill processes, introduce random input, create program faults and otherwise try to crash a program, persona or device.

*Biofeedback Filter Program						Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Biofeedback filters are software routines that monitor simsense signals and filter harmful feedback. Hackers specifically use biofeedback filters against attack programs in cybercombat and against dumpshock.

*Corrupt Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

A mix of Edit and Browse subroutines, Corrupt programs are designed to track down and demolish specific information in a node without actually deleting the files in which they are saved. The idea is that, since deleted files can be restored from back-ups, Corrupt edits the files to overwrite the targeted information while leaving the file intact, without making any indication of the alteration, so that the corrupted file is eventually backed up as well, making detection and recovery of the original more difficult.

*Decrypt Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Decrypt programs are designed to conduct a number of cipher-busting attacks – from pattern analysis to brute-force dictionary assaults to sophisticated mathematical tricks – to break into an encrypted system or service.

*Evasion Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Evasion programs hinder attack programs from successfully affecting your persona.

*Exploit Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Exploit programs are constantly evolving hacker tools specifically designed to take advantage of security flaws and weaknesses so that a hacker can gain unauthorised access to a node or program.

*Medic Program								Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Use Medic programs to repair Matrix damage inflicted on Personas and Devices. Though legitimate users sometimes use Medic programs to fix corrupted files, misbehaving programs and other errors, hackers use Medic to keep functioning after a bout of cybercombat.

*Snoop Program								Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

*Spoof Program								Restricted Licence*

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

*Stealth Program							Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Stealth is a clever hacker program that attempts to hide the hacker from other system processes. While it cannot make an icon completely undetectable, it makes the hacker seem innocuous by obfuscating their activities, erasing system tracks and mimicking authorised traffic. While it is not used for any action, Stealth hides the hacker from detection by the Firewall as they break into a system, as well as from Matrix Perception tests and Trace User attempts.

*Track Program								Restricted Licence*

Rating 1							500¥

Rating 2							1,000¥

Rating 3							1,500¥

Rating 4							3,000¥

Rating 5							4,500¥

Rating 6							6,000¥

Track programs systematically analyse a user’s connection and follow the datatrail back to the originating node. Track is commonly used as an intrusion countermeasure with the intent of identifying and locating a hacker or launching a counterattack, but it is also used to keep tabs on automated taxis and emergency service calls.
### **Custom Programs**

*Black Hammer								Forbidden Legality*

Rating 6							12,000¥

Black Hammer is a program that samples the command transactions between the target and their device and injects dangerous biofeedback responses into the target’s simsense interface. These aggravated signals may overload the target’s neural connections and in turn render them unconscious or cause death from stroke, heart failure, respiratory paralysis, aneurysm or neurotransmitter autotoxicity – and those are just a few of the possible effects. It is used with a Matrix Attack action.

*Blackout								Forbidden Legality*

Rating 6							9,000¥

Blackout is a non-lethal version of Black Hammer. It causes Stun damage to both hot sim and cold sim VR users. Like Black Hammer, it is used with the Matrix Attack action. It has no effect on programs, IC, sprites or AR users. Damage from Blackout does not overflow into the Physical Condition Monitor.

*Cat’s Paw								Forbidden Legality*

Rating 4							3,000¥

A low-offensive attack program that distracts the user instead of damaging the device they are using. Cat’s Paw is useful to prevent a user from performing Matrix actions while not bricking the device they may be using. This program fills the AR display or VR experience with annoying errors, spam pop-ups and pop-unders or other distracting garbage. On a successful Matrix Attack action, instead of doing damage, the program generates a negative dice pool penalty equal to 2 + the number of net hits on the Matrix Attack action.
### **Foci**
There are several categories of foci: Enchanting, Power, Qi, Sorcery, Spirit and Weapon.

*Enchanting Foci*

*Force 1*										5,000¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 2*										10,000¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 3*										15,000¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 4*										20,000¥	Licence Restricted

An alchemical focus adds its Force in dice to any Alchemical Tests.

An artificing focus adds its Force in dice to any Artificing Tests.

When a disenchanting focus is in contact with another artifact, the magician can add dice equal to its Force to the Disenchanting Test.

*Force 2*										40,000¥	Licence Restricted

An enchanting focus adds dice equal to its Force to Alchemy, Artificing and Disenchanting Tests.

A sorcery focus adds dice equal to its Force to Counterspelling, Ritual Magic and Spellcasting Tests.

Qi foci only work for adepts. They channel mana into your adept powers. A qi focus can be an object, like other foci, but can also be worked into a body modification, like tattoos, ritual scarring and piercings. Each focus is specific to a single adept power at a specific level. While the focus is active, you get the power contained in it, or if you already have the power, the focus’s levels are added to your own (if it’s a power with levels).

*Sorcery Foci*

*Force 1*										5,000¥	Licence Restricted

A ritual magic focus adds dice equal to its Force to Ritual Magic Tests as long as the category of magic is the same category as the focus.

A spellcasting focus adds dice equal to its Force to Spellcasting Tests as long as the category of magic is the same category as the focus.

*Spirit Foci*

*Force 1*										5,000¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 3*										15,000¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 4*										20,000¥	Licence Restricted

A summoning focus adds dice equal to its Force to summoning attempts as long as the targeted spirit is in the same category as the focus.

The banishing focus adds its Force to the limit of a magician’s Banishing Test as long as the target spirit is in the same category as the focus.

A binding focus helps a magician tie a spirit to them. The focus adds its Force in dice to the magician’s Binding Test as long as the spirit is in the same category as the focus.

*Weapon Foci*

*Force 1*										7,500¥	Licence Restricted

*Force 3*										22,500¥	Licence Restricted

When used in physical combat, it gives you its Force as a dice pool bonus on your melee Attack Test.


**<a name="_toc218024816"></a>AUGMENTATION**\

============================================
Cyberware and bioware augmentations are everywhere in 2075. For the rich, the poor and everyone in between, bodyshops on every street corner offer minor modifications at your convenience, legally and otherwise. Even the gang-bangers on those street corners might be equipped with cybernetic vision, hearing enhancements or datajacks. 
### **Cybersurgery and Recovery Time**
Getting cyberware and bioware installed hurts. When you have an augmentation implanted (after character creation), your Physical and Stun Condition Monitors each take damage from the procedure (more damage the more extensive and invasive the procedure). Most cyberclinics and body shops offer recovery rooms for patients to rest and heal up after cybersurgery but beware the sterility and cleanliness of the less-reputable chop shops.
### **Cyberware**
#### **Headware**
*Cyberskull									0.75 Essence	Legal*

*Obvious*								10,000¥		[4] Capacity

*Synthetic*							15,000¥		[2] Capacity

In fact, more of a shell than a full replacement, after all, the squishy parts inside aren’t being replaced. Cyberskulls can have other cyberwear installed within them. In addition, it provides an additional physical damage box on the Condition Monitor.

*Cyberskull, Partial								0.4 Essence	Legal*

*Obvious*								8,000¥		[4] Capacity

*Synthetic*							12,000¥		[2] Capacity

The partial cyberskull is another throwback classic that’s seeing a comeback. By upgrading one side of the skull with a large interface board, quite a few upgrades can be installed directly into it, rather than requiring difficult surgery repeatedly, but it is less invasive and far less dangerous than a full cyberskull.

*Datajack							1,000¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

A datajack gives you a direct neural interface (DNI), which can be handy in a lot of situations. It comes with a retractable spool of micro-cable (about a meter long) that lets you directly interface with any electronic device via a universal access cable. Datajacks are equipped with their own cache of storage memory for downloading or saving files. Two datajack users can string a fibreoptic cable between themselves to conduct a private mental communication immune to radio interception or eavesdropping. Most Use Device Actions can be triggered with a DNI Use Device Action instead (going from a Simple Action to a Bonus Action).

*[Alphaware] High Quality Datajack*			1,200¥		0.08 Essence	Legal

*Data Lock									0.1 Essence	Legal*

*Rating 1			(Firewall 1)*				1,000¥

*Rating 2			(Firewall 2)*				2,000¥

*Rating 3			(Firewall 3)*				3,000¥

*Rating 4			(Firewall 4)*				4,000¥

*Rating 5			(Firewall 5)*				5,000¥

*Rating 6			(Firewall 6)*				6,000¥

This special datajack is popular with couriers, spies, diplomatic aides and executive liaisons. Effectively, it turns the character in whom it is installed into a walking data safe. The data lock protects the data from anyone not authorised to access it (possibly including you). Data locks are not wireless enabled; they can only be accessed via universal data connector. In fact, the bearer of the implant doesn’t have mental access to the data – they’re only a carrier.

*False Face							20,000¥		0.5 Essence	Restricted Licence*

Intended for use by actors, shadowrunners quickly found other uses for the false face, resulting in it being restricted in most countries and corporations. The bones of the face are replaced with dozens of small ceramic plates that may be adjusted and rotated by micro-servos implanted beneath them. Combined with small reservoirs of gel that allow inflation or deflation of facial features, this allows the user to resculpt their face to a wide variety of versions possible with their metatype. False face provides a +4 dice pool bonus to a character’s Disguise Tests. Changing one’s face takes 1 minute of concentration and is somewhat painful.

*[Alphaware] Fine False Face*			25,000¥		0.4 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Smaller ceramic plates, more widely dispersed gel reservoirs and higher quality micro-servos but no reduction in the pain caused.*

*Fangs			STR(P)					200¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

*Fangs (Retractable)	STR(P)					500¥		0.15 Essence	Legal*

Fangs come in both retractable and non-retractable versions. Fangs are difficult to use as weapons – lower the user’s Physical Limit by 2 when trying to attack an aware target with fangs.

*[Alphaware] Tepes Retractable Fangs*			600¥		0.12 Essence	Legal

*For the true devotees.*

*Fibre-Optic Hair						100¥/10cm	0.1 Essence	Legal*

The original scalp hair (or facial hair) is removed and replaced with artificial hair composed of fibreoptic cabling. This hair is not only available in every imaginable colour, but is programmable, allowing for patterns, designs or scrolling effects that nature could never manage. From sparkling stars in a nightscape of black to an explosion of neon colours to a scrolling advert of your favourite hair salon, the only real limit is one’s imagination. Cost is based on length (to a maximum of 1m). The user may activate a downloaded colour pattern as a Use Device Action.

*[Alphaware] Fibre-Optic Hair*			120¥/10cm	0.08 Essence	Legal

*Now with in-built frizz control!*

*Horn Compartment						1,000¥		- Essence		Legal*

Similar to a tooth compartment but larger, the horn compartment gives a slick way to carry credsticks, RFID tags or other small items. As the with tooth compartment, it can be equipped to remove the enclosed items with either a wireless signal or a hidden catch.

*Horn Implants			STR(P)				400¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

*Horn Implants (Retractable)	STR(P)				1,000¥		0.15 Essence	Legal*

Synthetic horns come in a wide array of shapes and sizes, from curled troll horns to devil horns to single rhinoceros-style horns. Horns are usually installed in the skull, but some users implant rows of horns to form a “bone crest” along the head, neck and/or back. All horn implants are structurally braced for use in combat. Retractable “telescoping” models are also available to give users the advantage of surprise. Each two minor horns (similar to those of a goat) count as one implant, as do single larger horns (such as those of a rhinoceros or ram).

*Olfactory Booster								0.2 Essence	Legal*

*Rating 1*								4,000¥

*Rating 2*								8,000¥

*Rating 3*								12,000¥

*Rating 4*								16,000¥

This cybersnout enhances, identifies and records smells and can play them back later. The massively enhanced olfactory capabilities of a sniffer open up a while new world of sensory data to you – you’ll be able to sense things that ordinarily only a scent-hound would. You can smell people’s emotions in their sweat, traces of ammunition propellant, explosives or biological and chemical warfare compounds – the list goes on and on. A cut-off function allows you to completely ignore intense odours, possibly the most convenient feature for use in your daily life. Add the booster’s Rating as a dice pool modifier to your scent-based Perception Tests.

*[Alphaware] Hubert Olfactory Booster*		20,000¥		0.16 Essence	Legal

*Finer quality discernment of the high-end input with an even faster response time. For those who know that sometimes life is on the line.*

*Oral Slasher							750¥		0.25 Ess/3 Cap	Forbidden Legality*

A spool of pointed wire placed under the tongue, the oral slasher is more truthfully called the oral thruster, launched forward by compressed air to impale the target before being quickly rewound, not unlike a frog’s tongue, only more dangerous. With a range of only one metre, the slasher is a melee weapon covered by the Exotic Weapon Skill.

*Skilljack											Legal*

*Rating 1*								4,000¥		0.1 Essence

*Rating 2*								8,000¥		0.2 Essence

*Rating 3*								12,000¥		0.3 Essence

*Rating 4*								16,000¥		0.4 Essence

*Rating 5*								20,000¥		0.5 Essence

*Rating 6*								24,000¥		0.6 Essence

This headware interprets knowsofts and linguasofts for your brain so you can use them as though they were your own. It can also run activesofts but they only act similarly to Knowledge Skills unless you have skillwires. The total of all skills running on a skilljack cannot exceed its Rating x2 and the maximum Rating for a skill is the skilljack’s Rating. Starting skills from storage and stopping skills is a Bonus Action. You can’t use Edge with skills you have through a skilljack. If you have more than one skilljack, only one of them can operate at a time.

*Subvocal Microphone						250¥		0.05 Essence 	Legal*

The next best thing to telepathy is the ability to stage-whisper at any range. This implanted microphone lets you communicate via subvocalized speech. A -4 dice pool modifier is applied to Perception Tests to overhear you when you’re subvocalizing.

*Tooth Compartment						800¥		- Essence		Legal*

The oldest cyberware on the market, these hollow teeth come in storage and breakable models. The storage model is used to smuggle really, really tiny contraband, the size of a datachip or a really small RFID tag. Items can be removed with a wireless signal or hidden catch. The breakable model triggers a linked effect (such as starting a tracking signal or releasing deadly poison into your mouth – make sure you remember which is which!) with a wireless signal or it may trigger when you bite down hard on the tooth.

*Voice Amplifier							1,000¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

Go loud or go home. An in-built cybernetic amplifier for your voice. You can speak with an increased volume (up to 100 decibels) without strain.

*Voice Mask							2,000¥		0.1 Essence	Forbidden Legality*

A much-downgraded version of the voice modulator, the voice mask doesn’t allow for modification of the volume or frequency of the user’s voice, nor does it allow recording, rebroadcasting or replication of someone else’s voice. What it does, however, is use dissonant frequencies to totally distort the user’s voice and make it completely unrecognisable and useless for identification.

*Voice Modulator								0.2 Essence	Forbidden Legality*

*Rating 1*								5,000¥

*Rating 2*								10,000¥

*Rating 3*								15,000¥

*Rating 4*								20,000¥

This implant gives you perfect pitch and enormous vocal flexibility and distortion capabilities. You can speak with an increased volume (up to 100 decibels) without strain, shift your pitch to make perfect bird calls or mellifluous singing and, most importantly, uncanny vocal impressions. The modulator can also play back (and more or less perfectly imitate) a recorded or captured voice. Add the Rating of the modulator as a dice pool bonus for Impersonation Skill Tests.

#### **Eyeware**
*Cybereyes											Legal*

*Rating 1*				Capacity [4]*			2,500¥		0.2 Essence

*Rating 2*				Capacity [8]*			4,500¥		0.3 Essence

*Rating 3*				Capacity [12]*			8,500¥		0.4 Essence

*Rating 4*				Capacity [16]*			14,500¥		0.5 Essence

The basic cybereyes system features 20/20 vision for both eyes, an image link at no extra cost, as well as capacity for vision enhancements.

`	`*Image Link*										Legal

A standard upgrade, this lets you display visual information (text, pictures, movies the current time, etc.) in your field of vision. This is usually AROs but you can display pretty much whatever you want on it. You and your team can use it to share tactical and situational info in real time. An image link is what you need to truly “see” AR and participate in the modern world.

*Eye Laser System						2,000¥		3 Cap		Legal*

This miniaturised laser system is only available for cybereyes and may be upgraded with additional functionality with some minor hardware adjustments and software upgrades. The basic eye laser system features a “look-to-talk” system, allowing the user to communicate and transmit information via infrared laser to another character with an eye laser system or external laser talk gear. The laser transmits through one eye and receives through the other. This communication system has the advantage of being discreet and, unlike wireless radio, is immune to jamming and interception. The lasers must be immobile and pointed towards each other and fog, smoke or other conditions may affect the transmission. The eye laser may also be used to scan barcodes and other optical glyphs.

*Eye Laser Microphone						1,500¥		2 Cap		Restricted Licence*

The eye laser microphone can be used for surveillance purposes. This bounces a laser beam against a solid object like a windowpane, reads the vibrational variations of the surface and translates them into the sounds that are occurring on the other side of the surface. Use a Perception + Intuition [Device Rating] Test. Maximum range is 100 metres.

*Eye Laser Rangefinder						1,000¥		1 Cap		Legal*

The eye laser rangefinder emits a laser beam that is reflected off a target’s surface and picked up by a detector to calculate the exact distance.

*Eye-Light System – White Light					500¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal*

The eye light system involves a pair of miniscule, high-power but low-heat lights installed into the user’s cybereyes. The mechanism is attached to the forward inner wall of the eye, with a second, smaller pupil installed to allow it to shine out. The light has a range of two meters and allow for a person with low-light vision to see for a range of ten times that. The thin beam illuminates an area roughly the size of a sheet of paper or half a fuse box, allowing for a wide range of activities while leaving the hands completely free. Activating or deactivating the eye light system is a Use Device Action.

`	`*Red – Nightvision Saving Light*				600¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal

Rather than standard white light, this version illuminates the area in a red, nightvision saving light that is harder to detect from a distance.

`	`*Ultraviolet Light*						750¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal

Ultraviolet light, invisible to regular sight lights the area. The ability to see in ultraviolet light is sold separately.

*Eye Recording Unit						1,500¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

This connects to the user’s optical nerves (or cybereye) and records all data directly into storage (accessible by the user’s PAN).

*Flare Compensation						1,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

This protects you from blinding flashes of light as well as simple glare. It mitigates the vision modifiers for glares and reduces the penalty from flashing lights.

*Low-Light Vision						1,000¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal*

This allows you to see normally in light levels as low as starlight. It doesn’t help in total darkness, though.

*Microscopic Vision						1,500¥		0.2 Ess/3 Cap	Legal*

Take your lab with you, but don’t forget your slides! Microscopic lenses allow for refocusing of the eye to a massive magnification of tiny, tiny objects, up to 1000x their normal size. When microscopic lenses are active, the user’s eye is unsuitable for any other task but a Use Device Action allows the lens to be switched on or off. An item further away than 30 centimetres is beyond the focal ability of active microscopic lenses. When microscopic lenses are being used, in addition to the obvious use, they provide a +4 dice pool bonus on Perception tests to examine the material in question.

*Smartlink							3,000¥		0.2 Ess/3 Cap	Restricted Licence*

This accessory interacts with a smartgun system to project the weapon’s angle of fire into the user’s vision, centring red crosshairs where the user is pointing and highlighting perceived targets. The smartgun’s laser rangefinder also calculates and displays the distance to the target. Additional data from the weapon, such as the ammunition level, heat buildup and stress can also be displayed. Requires an Image Link.

`	`*Subdermal Induction Pad*					500¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Restricted Licence

Implanted in the palm, this allows the user to link with a smartgun system through their grip, rather than a hackable wireless connection.

*Thermographic Vision						1,500¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal*

This enables vision in the infrared spectrum, enabling you to see heat patterns. It’s a very practical way to spot living beings in areas of total darkness, to check if a motor or machine has been running lately and so on.

*Vision Enhancement										Legal*

*Rating 1**								4,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap

*Rating 2**								8,000¥		0.2 Ess/2 Cap

*Rating 3**								12,000¥		0.3 Ess/3 Cap

This sharpens a character’s vision at all ranges, providing visual acuity closer to that of the average hawk than that of the average metahuman. It adds its Rating as a dice pool modifier to your visual Perception Tests and their Limit.

*Vision Magnification						2,000¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal*

This zoom function digitally magnifies vision up to fifty times, allowing distant targets to be seen clearly. p177

#### **Earware**
*Cyberears											Legal*

*Rating 1*				Capacity [4]*			2,000¥		0.2 Essence

*Rating 2*				Capacity [8]*			5,000¥		0.3 Essence

*Rating 3*				Capacity [12]*			8,000¥		0.4 Essence

*Rating 4*				Capacity [16]*			11,000¥		0.5 Essence

Ordinarily, cyberears replace only the inner ear, although the whole thing can be replaced as well if you like. Cyberears offer hearing with normal ranges, a sound link and Capacity for modifications and enhancements.

`	`*Sound Link*

The sound link can play audio (recordings, movie soundtracks, music, etc.) from linked sources within the user’s PAN (or headware memory or datajack) directly into the user’s cyberears. A sound link is a common component of immersive AR environments, adding a sonic component.

*Antennae							500¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

With an extended antenna array, the user can send and receive wireless signals easier than without. Available in both retractable and fragile or non-retractable and sturdy options for the same cost, they are often, but not always, taken in pairs and come in a wide variety of designs, shapes and colours. The antenna array reduces Noise by 1 for the user.

*Audio Analyser							1,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

A simple bit of hardware that measures and identifies both pitch and timbre, audio analyser is quite useful for musicians and impersonators, but it can also allow eavesdropping of old touch-tone datapads. The audio analyser raises the Social limit by 1 for musical performances by the user.

*Audio Enhancement										Legal*

*Rating 1**								4,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap

*Rating 2**								8,000¥		0.2 Ess/2 Cap

*Rating 3**								12,000¥		0.3 Ess/3 Cap

Audio enhancement allows the user to hear a broader spectrum of audio frequencies, including high and low frequencies outside the normal metahuman audible spectrum. The user also experiences fine discrimination of nuances and can block out distracting background noise. Audio enhancement adds its Rating as a dice pool bonus and Limit.

*Balance Augmenter						5,000¥		0.1 Ess/4 Cap	Legal*

The balance augmenter enhances the inner ear’s natural balance mechanism. You receive a +1 dice pool bonus on all tests involving balance, such as climbing, walking across a narrow platform, landing after a jump and so on.

*Damper							2,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

This implant protects the user from sudden increases in sound as well as damaging sound levels. The damper adds a +2 dice pool bonus to resisting sonic attacks, including flashbangs.

*Increased Hearing Spectrum					2,000¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

A basic augmentation that expands the user’s hearing spectrum beyond the typical metahuman breadth of 20 Hz to 20 kHz as well as beyond typical audio enhancements. The user’s hearing extends as low as 5 Hz, into infrasonic sound and as high as 120 kHz into the ultrasonic. This allows the user to hear sounds outside the normal range, such as dog whistles or ultrasound-based motion detectors, which would otherwise go unnoticed. If combined with a device to create such sounds, such as a voice modulator, then a method of signalling or even communication can be employed that is difficult for those without the augmentation to listen in on.

*Sound Filter											Legal*

*Rating 1**								3,500¥		0.1 Essence/1 Cap

*Rating 2**								7,000¥		0.2 Essence/2 Cap

*Rating 3**								10,500¥		0.3 Essence/3 Cap

*Rating 4**								14,000¥		0.4 Essence/4 Cap

This lets you block out background noise and focus on specific sounds or patterns of sounds. It even includes speech, word and sound pattern recognition. Each Rating point lets you select a single sound group (such as the footsteps of a patrolling guard or the rotors of a distant helicopter) and focus on it. You only actively listen to one group at a time, but you can record the others for later playback or set them to triggered monitoring (such as sounding an alert if a conversation brings up a certain topic or if there’s a variation in the breathing pattern of a guard dog).

*Spatial Recogniser						4,000¥		0.1 Ess/2 Cap	Legal*

This hearing accessory pinpoints the source of a sound. You get a +2 dice pool bonus to your audio-based Perception Tests and their limit.

#### **Bodyware**

*Auto-Injector						500¥		0.05 Essence	Legal*

Originally, auto-injectors were devices that released medication into a person’s body either when needed or on a regular time schedule. It took the street about thirty seconds to realise that you could replace, say, insulin with combat drugs and suddenly you have a sneaky boosting technology. While the base auto-injector is designed to hold a single dose of a chemical, an auxiliary storage unit is often implanted to allow up to five additional doses. The auto-injector is normally refilled from an external port. Not that while different chemicals can’t be mixed in a single dispensary, multiple injectors may be implanted to create a veritable salad bar of chemical cocktails.

*Expanded Reservoir (+5 doses)*			250¥		0.05 Essence	Legal

*Balance Tail						2,000¥		0.25 Essence	Legal*

Largely having fallen out of favour for their bioware cousins, balance tails are cybernetic tails extended from the user’s spine, focused on improved stability and balance. The tail is controlled by a dedicated sub-processor at the base of the spine and is autonomous, often moving about on its own without the user’s awareness as it quietly compensates for natural motion. While the base tail is in the always-classic chrome, faux-fur cat tails are, by far, the dominant style. Tails must be at least knee-length to be functional, but most are slightly longer than the user’s legs.

The balance tail raises the user’s Physical limit by 1 for all tests requiring balance, such as climbing, jumping or running. It also raises the user’s Physical limit by one for purposes of resisting knockdown.

*Biomonitor						500¥		0.1 Ess/1 Cap	Legal*

While this is simply an implanted version of the standard biomonitor, its cybernetic natures allows it to integrate the user’s augmentations into calculations so that, for instance, a user’s bone structure will not read as damaged just because they have plastic implants. It provides constant updates in their personal PAN, making checking your vitals into a Bonus Action.

*Biowaste Storage Expansion								Legal*

*Rating 1**							500¥		0.1 Essence/1 Cap

*Rating 2**							1,000¥		0.2 Essence/2 Cap

*Rating 3**							1,500¥		0.3 Essence/3 Cap

*Rating 4**							2,000¥		0.4 Essence/4 Cap

*Rating 5**							2,500¥		0.5 Essence/5 Cap

*Rating 6**							3,000¥		0.6 Essence/6 Cap

What it says on the tin. Each Rating point allows the user to store an entire day’s worth of liquid and solid waste for later offloading via an access port.

*Bone Lacing*

*Plastic*		Armour & Body +1		Damage (STR+1) P		8,000¥		0.5 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Aluminium*	Armour & Body +2		Damage (STR +2) P	18,000¥		1 Essence		Restricted Licence

*Titanium*		Armour & Body +3		Damage (STR +3) P	30,000¥		1.5 Essence	Restricted Licence

Your bones are laced with lattice chains of reinforcing plastics or metals, improving their integrity and tensile strength (and adding to your body’s overall weight). Bone lacing comes in three types: plastic, aluminium and titanium – you can only have one installed at a time. It gives you extra Body for the purpose of Damage Resistance Tests, additional Armour (cumulative with other Armour, without adding to Encumbrance) and changes your unarmed combat damage. Bone lacing is incompatible with other augmentations that add to or alter your bones (such as bone density augmentation).

*[Alphaware] Plastech Superior Bone Lacing*		10,000¥		0.4 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Now less detectable on cyberware scanners and undetectable on MAD scanners.*

*[Alphaware] AAA Titanium Bone Lacing*		36,000¥		1.2 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Tougher than tough.*

*Breast Implants 2.0						2,000¥		0.2 Essence	Legal*

For those who change their looks as often as they change their underwear, modern science has stepped up and given us new breast-tech, allowing the owner to adjust to whatever size they want. Hidden gel reserves and reflexive synthskin allow you to go from A to DD, changeable with a simple wireless command. Ta-da!

The user may change the size of the implants as a Use Device Action.

*[Alphaware] KL Breast Implants 2.0*				2,500¥		0.16 Essence	Legal

*Now with nipple resizing as endorsed by Kathia Lynn!*

*Pair of Cyberfins						1,000¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

Retractable webs for the user’s hands or feet, cyberfins make swimming a breeze.

When active, increase the user’s Physical limit for Swimming Tests by 2 and the Swimming skill by +1.

A user may have one pair on their feet and another on their hands. Lastly, a user with a pair of cyberfins has their Swimming speed increased to 150% of normal or 200% with two pairs.

Note that engaged cyberfins make use of that limb difficult for fine motor work, lowering the user’s Physical limit or a held weapon’s accuracy by 1 for activities such as making repairs, typing, dancing and so on. Activating or deactivating cyberfins is a Use Device Action.

*Dermal Plating*

*Rating 1*								3,000¥		0.5 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Rating 2*								6,000¥		1 Essence		Restricted Licence

*Rating 3*								9,000¥		1.5 Essence	Restricted Licence

Hard plastic and ceramic fibre plates are bonded to the user’s skin. The plates are clearly visible and are even more obvious to the touch but they can be cosmetically stylised for colour and surface texture. Dermal plating gives you bonus Armour equal to its Rating (cumulative with other Armour, without adding Encumbrance). Dermal plating cannot be combined with other augmentations to the skin that provide armour, including orthoskin.

*[Alphaware] Dermatough Plating (Rating 3)*			11,000¥		1.2 Essence	Restricted Licence

*When you need to be tougher than the rest, think Dermatough.*

*Fingertip Compartment						2,000¥		0.1 Essence	Legal*

This compartment is hidden in the hollowed out last joint of one finger, with a catch that allows the fingernail to be lifted up as an access panel or the entire fingertip removed. A fingertip compartment allows the storage of micro-sized items, like an RFID tag, datachip or pill. Inserting or removing an object takes one Complex Action. Items held within are completely concealed and the compartment itself has Concealability -10.

*Gastric Neurostimulator					2,000¥		0.2 Essence	Legal*

A simple set of electro-stimulators that respond to nausea by correcting the stomach, inner ear or other affected areas with tiny electrical impulses, rendering the user immune to the effects of nausea or motion sickness. Quite popular with sailors, acrobats and those orbital-intended workers. The user is immune to Nausea.

*Grapple Gun							5,000¥		0.5 Essence	Restricted Licence*

This is an implanted version of the grapple gun. It can shoot a grappling hook up to 120 metres (the limit of its extreme range). (Ranges: Short 0-6m / Medium 7-24m / Long 25-60m / 61-120m.) It comes equipped with an internal winch to pull back the grapple (or pull up loads) Use the *Exotic Ranged Weapon – Grappling Hook* skill to shoot it. It doesn’t store any rope inside it, but you can attach an external rope before you shoot the grapple. Micro rope can support a weight of up to 100kg; standard and stealth ropes can support a weight of up to 400 kg. Reinforced rope can support a weight of up to 600kg.

*Internal Air Tank*

*Rating 1*								4,500¥		0.25 Essence	Legal

*Rating 2*								6,500¥		0.25 Essence	Legal

*Rating 3*								8,000¥		0.25 Essence	Legal

The internal air tank replaces part of one lung with a pressurised internal air reserve that allows you to hold your breath for up to (Rating) hours. This allows extended underwater operations and complete protection from inhalation-vector toxin attacks as long as you’re holding your breath. Activating or de-activating the tank is a Use Device Action. It can also be set to activate automatically if it detects the need for air. If linked to your PAN, you can always be aware of the tank’s exact air level and purity. Refilling the air tank with pressurised air through an intake valve (located under your ribcage) takes about five minutes per hour of air tank capacity needed, or you can refill it through six hours of normal breathing per hour of air tank capacity.

*Internal Router							15,000¥		0.7 Essence	Legal*

Using the body’s internal neural network as “wires”, the internal router allows the user’s cybernetics to communicate with one another as if they were wirelessly connected and, if expanded via a datajack or similar broadcast-enabled piece of cyberware, with the rest of the user’s gear.

*LED Tattoos											Legal*

*Small*								100¥+		0.05 Ess/1 Cap

*Medium*								500¥+		0.1 Ess/2 Cap

*Large*								1,000¥+		0.2 Ess/4Cap

LED tattoos have staged a surprising comeback. A simple LED display is implanted under the skin, bright enough to be seen through the dermal layer when active, vanishing from sight when inactive. Available in three general sizes – small (placed on a wrist, ankle or behind an ear), medium (covering much of a forearm or upper arm, the small of the back or over the heart) or large (covering most of the back or scalp) – LED tattoos combine the showcasing of one’s interests and expression of personality with the ability to remove or change those that are no longer quite so definitive. The ability to deactivate them further allows for someone to switch between club mode, where they fly their freak flag, and work mode, where they blend in with sedate corporate culture. It should be noted that there is some division between those with “real” tattoos and “light posers” who are unwilling to get proper ink done.

*Muscle Replacement*

*Rating 1	Cheap Charlie Muscles*					25,000¥		1 Essence		Restricted Licence

*Rating 2	Built Brick Muscles*						50,000¥		2 Essence		Restricted Licence

*Rating 3	Arnie Awesome Muscles*					75,000¥		3 Essence		Restricted Licence

Why take the time to exercise when you can just install a physique? Vat-grown synthetic muscles replace or augment your own and calcium treatments and skeletal reinforcement contribute to your overall strength. It increases both your Strength and Agility attributes by its rating. It cannot be combined with other augmentations to the muscles (such as muscle augmentation or muscle toner bioware).

*Nutrition Storage System*

*Rating 1*								500¥		0.1 Essence	Legal

*Rating 2*								1,000¥		0.2 Essence	Legal

*Rating 3*								1,500¥		0.3 Essence	Legal

An onboard reserve of tasteless food paste and water, the former released directly into your stomach, the later into your mouth and throat. Each Rating point allows for a day’s worth of food and water to be stored. The reservoirs are refilled through an external port and part of the user’s Lifestyle cost. This augmentation is not compatible with the elastic stomach genetech.

*Reaction Enhancers*

*Rating 1*								13,000¥		0.3 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Rating 2*								26,000¥		0.6 Essence	Restricted Licence

By replacing specific, isolated vertebrae of your spinal column with segments of superconducting material, your reactions to events become quicker. Add the Rating of reactions enhancers to your Reaction attribute (and remember to adjust Initiative and Physical limit accordingly). Reaction enhancers are incompatible with other enhancements to Reaction, except Wired Reflexes.

*[Alphaware] Elite Reaction Enhancers	(Rating 2)*		32,000¥		0.48 Essence	Restricted Licence

*For the Elite!*

*Skillwires*

*Rating 1*								2,000¥		0.1 Essence	Legal

*Rating 2*								4,000¥		0.2 Essence	Legal

*Rating 3*								6,000¥		0.3 Essence	Legal

Skillwires are a system of neuromuscular controllers that overlie the body’s natural nervous system; they are capable of aiding or completely overriding muscular movement, controlled by the “muscle memory” played through a skilljack. This system allows you to use activesofts with a rating up to your skillwire’s rating, but only if that activesoft is running on your implanted skilljack. Skillwires are incompatible with reflex recorder bioware.

*Skin Toner							8,000¥		0.5 Essence	Legal*

Gently weaving ruthenium polymer into the user’s skin and implanting a dedicated control system to watch over it, skin toner allows the user to select any shade of colour for their skin tone. The limited processor requires the entire body to be generally the same colour, minus some minor gradients for tanning, flesh density and so forth. The user may change skin colour with a Use Device Action.

*[Alphaware] Transformative Epidermis*				10,000¥		0.4 Essence	Legal

*This upgraded tech allows even finer control and allows freckle patterns!*

*Smuggling Compartments					7,500¥		0.2 Essence	Legal*

For items that won’t fit in a fingertip but that you still can’t afford to have found, smuggling compartments can be placed in part of the body that can be easily hollowed out/replaced. This includes ribs and the space between them, hip bones, shoulder blades and so forth. These compartments can allow the storage of small and mini-sized items of appropriate size and shape. The compartment has a Concealability of -10. Inserting or retrieving on object requires a Complex Action.

*Wired Reflexes*

*Rating 1*								30,000¥		2 Essence		Restricted Licence

*Rating 2*								140,000¥		3 Essence		Restricted Licence

This highly invasive, painful, life-changing operation adds a multitude of neural boosters and adrenaline stimulators in strategic locations throughout your body work to catapult you into a whole new world where everything around you seem to move in slow motion. Those with wired reflexes tend to be twitchy and even their regular movements may appear unusual. Each rating point of wired reflexes gives you +1 Reaction (and accompanying bonus to Initiative and Physical limit) and +1D6 Initiative Die. Wired reflexes cannot be combined with any other form of Initiative enhancement, except Reaction Enhancers.

*Reflex Trigger*						9,000¥		0.2 Essence

A reflex trigger is an accessory for wired reflexes, allowing the user to cybernetically turn the reflexes on or off as a Use Device Action. The wired reflexes and the reflex trigger must be installed simultaneously, as a package; the trigger cannot be retrofitted later. When turned off, the reflex trigger adds 1 to the threshold for tests to detect the wired reflexes with a cyberware scanner.

*Stepped Reflex Trigger*					11,000¥		0.2 Essence

Rather than completely turning off their wired reflexes, some users prefer to turn them down. This modification to the reflex trigger allows users to operate their wired reflexes at a lower level than the level at which they were purchased.

*[Alphaware] Renraku Redline Reflexes*				48,000¥		1.76 Essence	Restricted Licence

*Redline your reflexes because you know you can push it to the max. With stepped reflex trigger included!*

#### **Cyberlimbs**
In today’s world of transplant-friendly bioware, the use of cyberlimbs is sometimes viewed as crude and outdated. On the other hand, they are cheap and easy to service and upgrade, so in the end they became even more popular for the less fortunate. Since cyberlimbs are more capable than most natural limbs and you can load them up with all sorts of wiz tech, this kind of cyberware has stayed in high demand.

Cyberskulls and -torsos are considered cyberlimbs, although they are in fact shells rather than full replacements (or actual limbs).

Cyberlimbs have their own Strength and Agility Ratings. When a particular limb is used for a test, use the attribute for that limb (natural or cyber); in any other case, take the average value of all limbs involved in the task. If a task requires the careful coordination of several limbs, use the value of the weakest limb. The attributes of partial limbs (including cyberhands and -feet) may be enhanced, but their attributes only apply to tests directly involving those limbs). Cyberlimbs cannot hold any bioware, nor any cyber-implants that take up Essence rather than Capacity.

Cyberlimbs give you 1 extra damage box on your Physical Condition Monitor for each cyberlimb you possess (ignore hands and feet and partial limbs count for half a limb). They have Capacity, letting you add cyberweapons and other cyber systems that have a Capacity Cost [in brackets]. They can perform at superhuman levels with the right enhancements. Cyberlimbs can be dangerous even if they don’t have cyberweapons installed – their unarmed DV is (STR)P.

*Obvious Cyberlimbs:* These implants are immediately recognisable as artificial limbs unless you cover them with clothing. They are often chromed or matte colours but visibly mechanical in nature. Some folks like them glaringly obvious and outlandish, some find the artificiality repellent and disturbing. This can affect your social dealing in some circles, especially upper-crust society and the purist crowd.

*Synthetic Cyberlimbs:* Synthetic limbs are disguised as natural limbs. The face that they’re cybernetic gives them a -8 Concealability (the Cybertechnology skill may replace Perception for this test) when someone’s looking, but synthetic limbs are obviously artificial to the touch.

*Full Arm									1 Essence		Legal*

*Obvious		STR/AGI 3*					15,000¥		15 Capacity

*Obvious		STR/AGI 4*					25,000¥		15 Capacity

*Obvious		STR/AGI 5*					35,000¥		15 Capacity

*Obvious		STR/AGI 6*					45,000¥		15 Capacity

*Synthetic		STR/AGI 3*					20,000¥		8 Capacity

*Synthetic		STR/AGI 4*					30,000¥		8 Capacity
